A young boy carries a visibly-wounded, unconscious girl through a snowy path on his back. This girl is revealed to be his younger sister, Nezuko. He treks frantically through the snow and begs her to stay alive, vowing that her big brother would save her.
Tanjiro Kamado prepares to depart his home.
As New Year is about to arrive, Tanjiro Kamado prepares to leave his home, selling charcoal to put food on his family's table for the holiday. His siblings Hanako and Shigeru overhear him and beg to go as well, but their mother sternly refuses as they would only slow him down. Tanjiro calls out to his brother, Takeo, and asks him to chop the firewood while he's away, much to the latter's disappointment as he hints that he wanted to chop wood with his older brother. Tanjiro bids farewell to his mother and siblings as they remind him to stay safe. As he sets off, he runs into Nezuko, rocking their youngest sibling, Rokuta, to sleep. She mentions their younger siblings' attachment to Tanjiro since their father's death and bids him goodbye.
As he travels, he remarks that they have always made the most of their life, since it could quickly one day shift so suddenly. As Tanjiro arrives in the town, everyone is delighted to see him and immediately call him over to buy some of his charcoal. One of the villagers cries out to Tanjiro and asks him to take a whiff of a broken plate to figure out who the culprit was. The boy's keen sense of smell is able to detect that it was a cat at fault and not the villager who was being held responsible for it.
As the sun begins to set, Tanjiro begins his journey home but before he goes to ascend the mountain, an elder by the name of Saburo stops him on his travel, forbidding to let him from going back to the mountain as the sky turns dark. He tells him not to worry as his nose can quickly smell dangers, but the man insists he take refuge in his house for the night in case of a demon attack. Inside his hut, Tanjiro asks if demons could enter homes. Saburo answers so, informing him it is the job of Demon Slayers to protect them. Saburo, who lost his family to demons years ago, is pitied by Tanjiro, while remembering that his grandmother too had said something about demons to him before her death.
Nezuko begins to stir, revealing she is no longer human.
At dawn, Tanjiro departs from Saburo's residence and makes his way back. Outside his yard, he sees a bloodied Nezuko holding Rokuta lying on the snowy ground. Horrified, he goes to check the house and is shocked to see his home destroyed and everyone inside brutally killed. As Nezuko is the only one with warmth in her body, Tanjiro hurriedly carries her on his back to see a doctor. Questions begin to flood Tanjiro's mind as he wonders if a bear was responsible for the attack. The blizzard makes it difficult for him to breathe and he struggles to make his way to the town. Suddenly, Nezuko rears up, growling and with fangs in her mouth; she pulls back on Tanjiro and causes both of them to fall off a cliff. The thick snow protects Tanjiro from the fall.
He finds Nezuko standing upright and asks if she is okay, only to be suddenly attacked by her. Tanjiro is forced to jam his hatchet into her mouth to prevent getting bit as he realizes to his horror that Nezuko is now a demon. He questions why, since she was born human, despite her now smelling of death and blood. However, he remembers that she was lying over Rokuta and didn't have the blood of her family on her, noting that another scent was inside the house. She grows in size and gains strength, with Tanjiro struggling more to hold her back. He laments that his family has died brutally whilst he was away. Tanjiro starts attempting to appeal to what is left of his sister's humanity, encouraging her to stop and do her best to not give into being a demon. Eventually, she ceases her struggle and starts to cry; upon seeing his sister's tears, Tanjiro cries as well.
A swordsman attacks the demon Nezuko.
Suddenly, a swordsman strikes at Nezuko: Tanjiro rolls himself and Nezuko away to avoid the attack. The katana-wielding man asks why Tanjiro was protecting a demon. Although Tanjiro tells him that the demon is his sister, the man insists on killing her, before lunging forward and grabbing hold of Nezuko, too fast for Tanjiro to see. He states that it is his job as a Demon Slayer to kill them and prepares to behead her. Tanjiro begs for her life and claims she has not killed anyone, wondering why she was turned into a demon in the first place, only for the man to respond that since demon blood has enter her through injuries, she has transformed. He promises to make a cure but the Demon Slayer tells him becoming a demon is irreversible.
Giyu tests Tanjiro's resolve, questioning if he can truly save Nezuko.
Unwilling to let the last of his family die, Tanjiro kneels down and begs for Nezuko to be spared. The man grows angry and rebukes him for his weak resolve, stating that a weak person cannot avenge his family or return his sister into a human again. He demands that Tanjiro fight for something, claiming that demons may know how to change someone back but will not respect whining and crying, adding that he doesn't respect Tanjiro as well. Inside, the swordsman chastises himself for being late but refuses to dwell further. Despite knowing the great pain Tanjiro is experiencing, he begs the boy to keep his anger in his heart, as it will push him to do what he must.
While Tanjiro is left forlorn, the swordsman stabs Nezuko in the chest, causing her great pain. Tanjiro immediately throws a rock at him and charges. The man becomes angry over what was merely an emotionally-charged attack. He knocks Tanjiro unconscious but notices that he was not carrying his hatchet. He looks up into the sky and ducks out of the way of the falling hatchet, barely missing him. Through this carefully-planned assault by the young boy, the swordsman becomes aware of Tanjiro's resolve to protect his sister, willing to sacrifice even his own life in order to save her from him. While the swordsman is distracted, Nezuko breaks free of his hold and rushes to Tanjiro's motionless body. The swordsman curses himself for letting his guard down, expecting Nezuko to devour her brother.
However, she instead defends her unconscious brother, using her own body to shield him. The man recalls many a time that someone too had said the same about their demon-turned relative, only to be eaten since demons will even feed on family members. Seeing her injuries, he notes that she is spending energy to heal and yet refrains from killing Tanjiro. Realizing that these siblings are different, he opts to spare Nezuko, sheathing his katana and knocking her unconscious instead. As he is unconscious, Tanjiro dreams of his mother and siblings surrounding him; she apologizes for leaving him and entrusts Nezuko to his care.
Tanjiro buries his deceased family members.
Tanjiro wakes up with tears in his eyes, seeing Nezuko with a bamboo muzzle in her mouth to prevent her from biting him, laid unconscious but alive beside him. Having waiting for him to awaken, the swordsman appears behind a tree and asks them to look for an elder named Sakonji Urokodaki, who lives at the foot of Mount Sagiri, and to tell him that Giyu Tomioka sent them. Finally, he advises Tanjiro to not bring his sister out in the sun, before disappearing. Tanjiro buries the members of his family beside their house while Nezuko looks on. The Kamado siblings take each others' hands and starts on their journey to look for Sakonji.
Following Giyu's advice to keep Nezuko away from the sun, Tanjiro opts to buy a basket from a nearby farmer to protect her in the day. The farmer offers to give it for free since it is damaged but Tanjiro insists on paying. Again, he refuses money and adds that he can take the straw and bamboo for free. Tanjiro stubbornly wants to give him the money and the farmer annoyedly denies payment. Tanjiro slaps coins into his hand and thanks him, while the farmer yelps in pain. After repairing it, Tanjiro finds Nezuko has dug herself into a dirt tunnel, her scared expression showing her great reluctance to let sunlight touch her.
Unsure if she can fit, or even understand him, Tanjiro slowly asks if she could shrink herself similar to how she previously grew in size. Eventually, Nezuko does as Tanjiro asks and fits inside. With the basket on his back, Tanjiro sets out to Mount Sagiri. He finds a woman and asks for directions. She tells him the mountain is across another but is worried since it is now dark. Tanjiro reassures her that he will be safe.
As night falls, Tanjiro and Nezuko find a small temple hut in the woods and decide to look inside. As they enter, Tanjiro smells blood and worries about the possibility of a traveler being injured, rushing into the building. However, he instead finds a demon feasting upon the three dead residents. The demon shoots the siblings a glance and warns them that this is his feasting grounds. Upon seeing the bloodied bodies, Nezuko starts to salivate and Tanjiro goes into a state of shock at his first encounter with a man-eating demon.
The demon suddenly realizes that Tanjiro is human and rushes out of the temple to kill him. Tanjiro uses his hatchet to slash the demon by the neck, fending him away, but the wound immediately begins to heal. The demon proceeds to outspeed the boy and pins him onto the ground with his agility and strength. Before the demon can kill Tanjiro, Nezuko, who had been fighting the urge to eat the bodies, comes to her brother's aid and kicks his head clean off from his neck while Tanjiro watches, shocked over her unexpected new ability to kill.
The Temple Demon's body attacking Nezuko.
Tanjiro fighting the Temple Demon's head.
However, the demon's body continues to attack Tanjiro despite being beheaded, prompting Nezuko to give the headless body another kick. The severed head yells at Tanjiro, asking why a demon would travel with a human. He runs to grab Nezuko, distracting her and Tanjiro while growing another pair of arms from the detached head. He charges at Tanjiro but the boy proceeds to headbutt and pin him onto a nearby tree with his hatchet handle.
Tanjiro runs off into the forest to look for Nezuko, finding her under attack from the headless body as it continues to kick her dangerously close to a cliff's edge. He tackles the body off the cliff, being narrowly saved by Nezuko and making the headless body fall straight onto the ground below. Although the impact from the fall of his body causes the demon great pain, enough to knock him unconscious, it does not kill him.
The siblings return to the demon's head pinned by the tree and Tanjiro draws out a small knife, intending to end the demon's life. However, despite knowing that it will save the lives of others, he hesitates to kill it. Enough time in his hesitation passes for a person wearing a strange mask to approach him from behind, telling him that the knife that he holds cannot kill the demon.
Sakonji receiving the message from Giyu.
An old man wearing a tengu mask receives a letter from a crow sent by Giyu. Giyu states that a young boy whose family was slaughtered by a demon is on his way to meet him, wanting to become a Demon Slayer. Within the letter, Giyu additionally explains the boy's sister was turned into a demon; however believing she will not harm humans. He also observes that the boy possesses the same sharpened sense of smell as Sakonji does and requests that he train him, believing he could potentially grow to become the old man's successor.
Remembering this letter, the man now looks at Tanjiro as he is about to finish off the demon he has just restrained with a small knife. Tanjiro notes his strange mask, remembering how he never noticed the man's presence at all as his footsteps were so light. The boy asks him on the proper course of action but the man tells him not to trust what others say, claiming he must solve this alone.
Tanjiro spots a rock nearby and decides that instead of the knife, assuming he could use the rock to crush the demon's skull repeatedly until it eventually dies. However, before he is able to act, he feels a pang of sympathy imagining how much pain the demon would suffer and tries to think of a less painful method to kill it in one blow. Upon detecting Tanjiro's hesitation, Sakonji realizes Tanjiro's scent is overflowing with empathy, reluctance, and kindness even towards a demon, berating Giyu in his mind as he believes that Tanjiro isn't a suitable candidate. The demon then awakens and weakly tries to grab at Tanjiro.
Sakonji slapping Tanjiro for hesitating.
As Tanjiro continues to hesitate with making a move, the first rays of sunlight appear and instantly burn the demon to ashes, causing Tanjiro to realize why Nezuko dislikes the sun so much: Nezuko, inside the temple, has crawled back inside her basket to avoid the sunlight. Meanwhile, Sakonji gives the deceased a proper burial within the outside area. When Tanjiro approaches the man, he introduces himself as Sakonji Urokodaki but before Tanjiro has the opportunity to properly introduce himself and his sister, Sakonji questions Tanjiro on what he would do if his sister ever devoured a human being. Tanjiro pauses before answering and Sakonji slaps him, reprimanding him for being too hesitant to give a quicker response.
He tells Tanjiro that in the event of his sister ever eating a human being, he should kill her and then kill himself, as he conveys that is the reality of travelling with a demon-turned sibling. Sakonji firmly claims he must never let Nezuko take an innocent life, asking if Tanjiro understands him. Understanding the fundamental threat and danger of what he is doing, Tanjiro acknowledges. With his answer, the man tells him he will test his resolve to see if he is fit to be a Demon Slayer.
Tanjiro running after Sakonji.
Running in the middle of the day, Sakonji's speed makes it difficult for Tanjiro to follow after him. As he is running, Tanjiro feels sorry for Nezuko as she is being jostled around inside the basket. He recalls Nezuko always being patient whilst enduring hardships throughout her whole life. For the sake of their siblings, Nezuko had refused to buy new clothes in order to buy more food for them instead. Tanjiro firmly vows to turn her back into a human and give everything to her with the intent of redeeming himself for the things he is unable to do now for his deceased siblings. They soon reach a hut and Tanjiro breathlessly asks whether he had passed the test but Sakonji tells him that the test has only just begun, ordering him to ascend the mountain. Upon hearing these words, Tanjiro is dumbfounded but complies.
After leaving Nezuko in the hut, the pair head up the mountain. After a while, Tanjiro feels that his legs are tired to the point where he is unable to move them and his head grows dizzy. Upon reaching a certain point, Sakonji reveals to Tanjiro that the test is for him to reach the bottom of the mountain to where his house is, declaring he will not wait until dawn for him this time as Sakonji then vanishes within the haze. Surprised that the test is so simple, Tanjiro believes his sense of smell would make it a breeze and begins following Sakonji's scent. However, just as he takes a step, Tanjiro's foot gets caught into a trap which launches small rocks towards him. He then falls into a hidden pitfall, before he then accidentally triggers another trap right after crawling out, releasing a tied log that hits him from behind.
Tanjiro successfully returns.
Tanjiro grasps the possibility that he would not be able to reach the foot of the mountain by dawn if he continues to get caught in these traps. Moreover, the mountain's air is thinner than where he had lived before, causing him to have difficulties of breathing normally. Feeling desperate, Tanjiro wonders if he could truly make it back in time before steadying himself and tells himself with determination that he must make it back. By adjusting his breathing and concentrating, he attempts to smell out the distinctly different hidden human traps in the surroundings. Even so, he is not agile enough to avoid all of them.
Meanwhile, by the foot of the mountain, Sakonji places a blanket over the sleeping Nezuko. He suddenly hears some noise by his door and sees it open to discover a bloodied and battered Tanjiro panting heavily. As he slumps down to the ground, Tanjiro states he successfully made it back. As the morning sun begins to rise, Sakonji informs Tanjiro that he has now acknowledged him as his student.
Sakonji explains to Tanjiro that the Demon Slayer Corps consists of several hundred members, and despite it not being recognized by the government, they have fought demons for a long time and continue to battle demons today. However, its leader is shrouded in mystery.
He goes on to tell Tanjiro more information about demons. While it is unsure how they began to appear, there are things that are known with certainty; they must eat humans in order to survive and they have special abilities, such as being able to regenerate wounds when they're physically injured. Others can even change form or use special powers. The only way they can be destroyed is through exposure to sunlight or by decapitation with a specialized blade. The organization of the Demon Slayers have continued to hunt them with their mortal selves across a number of generations.
Sakonji then introduces his role as one of the many 'cultivators', individuals who train and furnish swordsmen with a variety of techniques and skills. He informs Tanjiro that if anyone desires to join the ranks of the Demon Slayers, they must first survive an event known as Final Selection, held at Mount Fujikasane. Sakonji reveals to Tanjiro how he will be the only one to decide if he is qualified enough to participate in Final Selection.
After numerous descents down Mount Sagiri, Tanjiro has grown stronger and his sense of smell has sharpened. However, he also discerns the traps are becoming alarmingly more dangerous at the same time, coming to the assumption of whether Sakonji's real motive is actually trying to kill him. When he makes a descent while holding a katana, it gets in the way and causes him to be ensnared in the traps again. Next, he is taught skills of the sword, swinging it repeatedly and Sakonji explaining how slicing along the direction of the blade is the way to make a direct cut, as it may break when used incorrectly.
Tanjiro trains with Sakonji.
Then, he is taught to get back up after a fall, with Sakonji repeatedly tripping him over for a whole day. He then instructs Tanjiro to attack him armed whilst he is bare-handed. The old trainer effortlessly flips him into the air and defeats his student with ease. He is then taught breathing forms, but when told to take a deep breath, Tanjiro's long inhale is answered by a slap in the stomach for using  the incorrect method.
Tanjiro trains for six months, but in that time, Nezuko continues to remain in a deep sleep. Sakonji calls on a doctor to comes by and look at her, but he finds nothing wrong with the demon. Anxious by the possibility of finding her dead, Tanjiro steels himself and decides to train harder.
Sakonji tells Tanjiro to split the boulder and prove himself.
After a full year of training, Sakonji tells Tanjiro that he has nothing else to teach him. Taken aback, Tanjiro notes the amount of time that has passed since their arrival. Sakonji tells the boy to continue improving his techniques and challenges Tanjiro to split a huge boulder in half in order to prove his worth and participate in Final Selection. Tanjiro starts to panic, as the task at hand seems impossible with a mere blade, but from that day onwards, Sakonji ceases to teach Tanjiro new skills.
As another six months passes, while his technique and body has gotten more refined, Tanjiro is still unable to split the rock no matter how hard he practices. Confused at his fruitless efforts and disheartened, he yells in frustration, to which a voice demands him to silence himself. Surprised, Tanjiro observes that the voice came from a person wearing a fox mask, perched on top of the boulder, a person who did not have a scent nor a presence. The masked boy tells Tanjiro to bear his suffering like a man would and attacks him using a wooden blade, which Tanjiro clumsily blocks. The boy notes the extent of Tanjiro's weaknesses, deeming him unsuitable to be a Demon Slayer.
The boy with a fox mask challenges Tanjiro to a fight, to which he declines as the stranger is only wielding a wooden sword, whilst Tanjiro has with him a real sword. The boy laughs at Tanjiro for believing he had a chance and declares that as someone who had succeeded in splitting the boulder, he wouldn't be hurt by someone weaker. Shocked by learning the boulder can be split, Tanjiro is beaten down by the stranger's superior technique, who continues to admonish him for only remembering Total Concentration Breathing as a fact without understanding it, much less using it.
Makomo appears.
Tanjiro claims he has tried to do so but the boy tells him that trying and doing it is not the same. Ordering him to attack with all his strength, Tanjiro swings at the stranger, who dodges and strikes him in the chin, knocking him unconscious. With his opponent defeated, the masked boy turns his attention to a girl entering the forest, only telling her, "I'll leave the rest to you".
Tanjiro sees the girl as he awakens and asks her if she had witnessed the fight. Tanjiro states to her how he wishes to be as skilled as the boy someday, stunned by his unique abilities. The girl replies that he will indeed be able to master those techniques one day, claiming she will be there to witness his strength. Tanjiro requests for her name, thinking to himself that the girl is cute. She introduces herself as Makomo and the boy with the fox mask as Sabito.
Over time, Makomo acts as Tanjiro's teacher to aid him in correcting his sword postures, bad habits, and breathing techniques. When Tanjiro asks why she was willing to teach him, she only replies, "We really like Urokodaki", to Tanjiro's confusion. Makomo also informs Tanjiro that she and Sabito are not siblings; they were orphans taken in by Sakonji along with many children that are currently watching him.
Makomo teaches him the importance of Total Concentration Breathing. It accelerates blood flow and increases the body's temperature, enabling them to match a demon's strength. By expanding the lungs, one can force much air into the body and become enhanced in strength. Tanjiro is perplexed by this understanding; when asking Makomo how it is possible, she only says, "You must train so hard that you could die. Basically, I don't think there's anything else you can do". Even after excessively training over time, to the point where his arms feels as if they may be ready to fall off along with his heart and lungs burning within his chest, Tanjiro is still unable to defeat Sabito.
Sabito's mask breaks, revealing his face.
Six months pass since Tanjiro has met Sakonji's students, culminating in a final spar with Sabito now armed with a real blade. A determined and changed Tanjiro announces to Sabito that this is the day he will win. In a simple head-on contest, the stronger and faster blade wins: Tanjiro and Sabito clash but the battle is over in an instant when Tanjiro becomes the one to strike first. Cutting through Sabito's fox mask, it falls off to reveal a both sad and relieved blissful smile from Sabito directed at him. A smiling Makomo tells him: "Win Tanjiro... against them too".
Sabito and Makomo disappear in a haze as Tanjiro realizes that his sword, believing had cut through Sabito's mask, actually sliced the boulder in half.
Sakonji informs his student of a crucial piece of information about defeating demons. He points out that they must be decapitated at the neck and that it can only be done with a special blade called a Nichirin Sword.
Sakonji giving Tanjiro his blessing.
Tanjiro realizes that his training with Makomo has enabled him to detect the Opening Thread: a scent he follows to guide his blade towards his opponent's neck. Sakonji enters the clearing and informs him that he had no intention of sending Tanjiro to Final Selection. He could not bear to watch another child die and was certain the boulder could not be sliced. Acknowledging his student as remarkable, he pulls him into a hug and asks him to return from Final Selection safely, as his sister and himself will wait for him.
Before setting off, Tanjiro receives a hand carved warding mask which looked similar to the ones worn by Sabito and Makomo, from Sakonji and says goodbye to a still sleeping Nezuko. He bids his trainer farewell, entrusting him to care for Nezuko, Sabito, and Makomo while he is away. Sakonji is left astonished that Tanjiro is somehow able to recall the names of "those deceased children", questioning how he knew who they were.
Arrival at Final Selection.
Arriving to the Final Selection at Mount Fujikasane, Tanjiro admires the wisteria flowers glistening the area as he climbs up the stairs, since they do not bloom at this time of the year. Once he reaches the top, he encounters a large number of young swordsmen waiting to participate in the event. Two curators organizing the event inform the students that the mountain contains demons captured alive by Demon Slayers, and due to the blooming wisteria surrounded around the foot of the mountain they are imprisoned inside the forest because of their hatred of its scent. However, the wisteria only reaches half way up its slope, and past the top where they are, demons are free to roam about and hunt. The applicants must survive there for seven days to pass Final Selection.
Once the selection begins, Tanjiro immediately encounters two demons who bicker over the right to kill and eat Tanjiro. As they both charge at him, he utilizes Water Breathing, Fourth Form: Striking Tide and detects the Opening Thread, successfully defeating the demons simultaneously.
The deformed demon that Tanjiro encounters.
As he takes a moment to pray for the demon's souls, he is caught off guard by an overwhelming stench, and the screams of a applicant running away. When he turns to face the sound, he witnesses a large deformed demon chasing the swordsman while carrying another boy by the throat. As the boy runs, the demon suddenly manifests a gigantic arm that grabs the boy by the leg, pulling him into the air. Tanjiro stands in fear but wills himself to use his skill to help save the boy. Before the demon is able to eat the him, Tanjiro intervenes by using Water Breathing, Second Form: Water Wheel to slice one of the limbs off of the demon, who glares back at Tanjiro and comments, "Another of my dear foxes has come!"
In the forests of Mount Sagiri, at the site of Tanjiro's sliced boulder, Sabito and Makomo converse about the boy they have taught. Makomo worriedly asks if Tanjiro will be able to 'do it'. Sabito is unsure and remarks that no amount of effort is to much.
The morphed demon asks Tanjiro what Meiji emperor now sits on the throne. When Tanjiro answers that the imperial family is now the Taisho, the demon roars in anger over being imprisoned for so long, new dynasties have occurred. He curses Sakonji Urokodaki out loud, and when Tanjiro asks how he knows of his trainer, he replies it was Sakonji himself who imprisoned him on Mount Fujikasane 47 years ago, during the Keio era of the Edo Period. Tanjiro is shocked, with the applicant he saved claiming he is lying, stating that the demons of Final Selection are ones who have only killed 2-3 people. The demon replies he has survived for so long by eating 50 of them.
The Hand Demon gloats over killing Sakonji's students.
Tanjiro suddenly remembers Sakonji's advice that a demon's strength is equal to its number of human victims. It begins to count to 14 and suddenly points at Tanjiro, claiming he is the fourteenth student of Sakonji he has encountered, having devoured the previous 13. He mentions two that he will never forget: one was a boy with peach colored hair and a scar on his mouth, the most powerful student he has faced, and the other was a small girl who made up for her lack of size and strength with extreme agility.
He adds that by knowing the texture of the warding mask they wear, he can identify them as Sakonji's students and devour them in revenge, claiming that he might as well had fed them to him. Finally, he mentions that when he told Makomo this, she flew into a rage and couldn't focus, leading him to rip her apart.
The demon strikes an erratic Tanjiro from the side.
Enraged, Tanjiro lunges towards the morphed demon, slicing away its arms erratically. Sabito, sensing his anguished fighting, tells him to even out his breathing and forget about them. The boy is then struck by a stray arm from the side and slams into a tree, breaking his mask. The applicant he had saved sees him about to die and runs away to escape. Before the demon can grab him, Tanjiro sees a vision of Shigeru begging him to wake up.
He avoids the demon's grasp barely and continues slicing away its arms. He senses a scent from below and leaps up to avoid more arms from grabbing him, surprising the demon. It tries to punch him with a giant arm but Tanjiro headbutts it to deflect the blow. Seeing he has escaped his hold, the demon remains unfazed, remembering that his neck is so tough, even Sabito was unable to slash through.
Tanjiro gets close and senses the Opening Thread. When Makomo fears that Tanjiro will die too, Sabito states that it is not certain whether he can win or lose, but what is undisputable is that the boulder Tanjiro had managed to sliced is the largest one anyone has ever managed to accomplish.
Tanjiro then uses Water Breathing, First Form: Water Surface Slash and cuts through the neck of the giant demon.
A younger Sakonji Urokodaki.
As Tanjiro lunges forward to kill the morphed demon, he suddenly remembers experiencing the same feeling when he was defeated by Sakonji Urokodaki. His blade cuts through its thick neck, defeating it.
As the demon's head falls to the ground and his body begins to disintegrate to ash, he curses Tanjiro for killing him. Unable to turn his head away, he laments that he will witness the face of a disgusted Demon Slayer as the final thing he would ever see. To his surprise, Tanjiro looks at him with a sad expression on his face. Seeing this reminds him of when he was once a scared boy who always asked for his brother's hand, before remembering that he had eaten him after becoming a demon.
The demon's body grows a hand extended to Tanjiro, who smells the scent of sadness from within it. He gently holds it and prays that during reincarnation, this demon would no longer become one, as the severed head begins to cry. In the afterlife, the demon is turned into a young boy holding his older brother's hand. In the forests of Mount Sagiri, the souls of Sakonji's fallen students disappear in the mist, finally put to rest. Despite this, Tanjiro believes that if he had died, his soul would be with Nezuko's and Sakonji's.
Two survivors of Final Selection.
After seven days, the survivors of Final Selection meet at the mountain peak's shrine again. Tanjiro is shocked to find only four of them have lived, since there were nearly 20 of them in the beginning, and he laments not seeing the applicant he had saved previously. The twins who welcomed them to the selection congratulate the survivors. One boy laments his survival as he believed he would die during it, while another boy asks for his katana. A girl among them quietly admires a butterfly instead.
The twins inform the survivors that they will be issued a uniform and have their ranks engraved, of which there are ten: Mizunoto, Mizunoe, Kanoto, Kanoe, Tsuchinoto, Tsuchinoe, Hinoto, Hinoe, Kinoto, and Kinoe. All survivors are given the rank of Mizunoto. The boy of earlier asks for his katana again, to which the twins respond that they will instead choose their ore now but the blades are to be completed two weeks later. They are then assigned a Kasugai Crow for communication, though the scared boy has a sparrow instead.
Tanjiro stopping the quarrelsome boy.
Angered, the quarrelsome survivor swats away his crow and grabs one of the twins by the hair, demanding his sword now. Tanjiro grabs his arm and demands he let go, threatening to break it. When the boy implores him to try, Tanjiro tightens his grip, hurting him into pulling away. Afterwards, they are presented with the ores of their blades.
At an unknown location, a man is informed by a Kasugai Crow that five have survived Final Selection. He wonders what kind of swordsmen they may become.
After surviving Final Selection, an exhausted Tanjiro walks back to Mount Sagiri, using a stick to support himself on his trek back to his trainer's hut. He laments his inability to gather information from at least eight demons, who did not answer his questions and tried to kill him, apologizing to Nezuko for his ill-fated optimism and failure.
Tanjiro reunites with Nezuko and Sakonji.
As night falls, he finally makes it back to Sakonji's hut. To his surprise, the door is kicked down and Nezuko walks out onto the yard. Seeing her awake for the first time in two years, he calls out to his sister and she runs to him. Tanjiro tries to race down to meet her but falls down due to his exhausted state. As he gets up, Nezuko reaches around and pulls him into a hug, while Tanjiro cries and holds her close, asking why she was asleep for so long. Sakonji then appears and embraces the siblings as tears fall from his mask, happy that a student of his has finally come home.
Fifteen days later, a man with unusual clothes and a hat lined with furin appears in Sakonji's residence. He introduces himself as Haganezuka and states that he has forged the sword of Tanjiro Kamado. Tanjiro says he is the recipient but Haganezuka puts down his Nichirin Sword onto the ground to unwrap it, ignoring Tanjiro's offer to come inside. He explains that the iron and sand used to forge it absorb sunlight, and it originates from a mountain that is constantly bathed in light. Inside his hut, Sakonji is annoyed that Haganezuka is speaking his mind without the consideration of others.
Haganezuka, Tanjiro's swordsmith, arrives to deliver his blade.
Suddenly, he turns to face Tanjiro, who is shocked to see him wearing a hyottoko mask. He calls Tanjiro a 'child of brightness', though he attempts to correct him by saying he is actually the son of Tanjuro and Kie. Haganezuka points out that he is talking about his red hair and eyes, saying he must come from a family that works with fire, surprising him. He turns to Sakonji and states that it would mean his blade would turn red.
Inside, Tanjiro prepares to unsheathe his blade for the first time. Haganezuka mentions that Nichirin Sword are also known as 'color-changing sword' as they do so with each wielder. Upon revealing the blade, Tanjiro watches as it turns black. Hearing Sakonji's and Haganezuka's reaction, the former puts his student at ease by pointing out that a black blade is simply uncommon, not a symbol of bad luck. However, Haganezuka is less than pleased, as he had hoped to see a red sword, and proceeds to attack Tanjiro.
Tanjiro's Kasugai crow interrupts the dispute to inform Tanjiro to disembark on his first mission, to resolve the mystery of girls disappearing night after night in a neighboring town.

As Tanjiro embarks on his mission as an officiated Demon Slayer, he remembers information provided to him by Sakonji. Nichirin Swords change color according to their users, but so little is known about swordsmen with black blades, it is believed they don't progress far. His uniform is made of a special breathable fabric that is waterproof and fire-resistant, as well as strong enough to repel the claws and teeth of a weak demon. Before leaving, he is given a new box by Sakonji for carrying Nezuko during the day, made with lighter stronger wood and lacquer for durability. He also mentions his idea that perhaps Nezuko sleeps to gain strength as an alternative to eating humans.
Tanjiro questions Kazumi about Satoko's disappearance.
As he walks through the town assigned as his mission, he notices a dishevelled man in the crowd. The man, Kazumi, is pitied by the folk as he was with the latest victim, Satoko, when she disappeared. Tanjiro questions him and Kazumi takes the Demon Slayer to where she vanished. Though he believes the boy will dissuade him, Tanjiro fully supports his idea that she disappeared and kneels to the ground, detecting the faint scent of a demon. Watching him investigate, Kazumi remembers when he had told Satoko's parents of what had happened, and her father had beaten him for blaming her disappearance as her simply vanishing.
As night approaches, a girl inside her house prepares to go to sleep. Lying in her futon, she sadly wonders on the whereabouts of the missing girls and hopes they are alright. Suddenly, her bedroom floor transforms into a dark puddle and demonic arms grab her from beneath; the girl is unable to scream and is dragged into the dark murk.
Tanjiro suddenly runs away, causing Kazumi to follow him as he explains that the scent is now stronger and that a demon is nearby by. He leaps up onto the rooftops to get a better view of the town and a stunned Kazumi realizes that the rumors of demons and the Demon Slayers are true. Tanjiro gets down and, detecting where the scent is strongest, stabs his blade into the ground, causing murky water to spurt out. He sees something in the water and grabs the girl, pulling her away from the demon.
Tanjiro meets the Swamp Demon.
From the puddle emerges a horned demon, causing Tanjiro to realize that it possesses a Blood Demon Art, remembering Sakonji's advice that they are supernatural abilities belonging to certain demons. He questions the demon about the missing girls but it instead grinds its teeth in anger and disappears. Entrusting the girl to Kazumi, he senses the scent approaching but is shocked to see three demons. Thinking quickly, he uses Water Breathing, Eighth Form: Waterfall Basin, hitting all three targets at once.
Before preparing for his first mission, Sakonji informs Tanjiro that only one demon has blood that is able to transform someone into a demon. It was the first demon to ever exist, doing so over a thousand years ago. It was the demon that killed his family and perhaps the only one who knows how to reverse a transformation. The demon's name is Muzan Kibutsuji.
Despite his attempt to strike all three demons at once, Tanjiro's attacks fails to hit its weak spots. He notes that they all have the same scent and surmises that they are clones of the same demon. Despite the trouble of protecting two people from three demons, he remembers knowing to ask them about information regarding Muzan Kibutsuji.
The Swamp Demon angered at Tanjiro.
When one clone tries to grab Kazumi, Tanjiro flips back and uses Water Breathing, Second Form: Water Wheel. He fails again to cut deeper than he had hoped and the demon escapes him. Suddenly, the clone angrily demands he stop interfering with his hunt, claiming that since the girl is now 16, she will taste worse. Another clone emerges and calms the first, claiming that he has already devoured much victims and that he is satisfied. Kazumi demands the demon let Satoko go when the last clone appears behind him.
He opens his robe to reveal a large collection of hairpins, telling him that if hers is in the bunch, she was already devoured. Kazumi, upon seeing Satoko's ribbon among them, begins to cry, while Tanjiro grows enraged at the number of lost lives, remembering the pain of losing his family and Nezuko's transformation. A clone then tries to attack Tanjiro but he dodges away from the blow and cuts off its arm, though he fails again to hit its neck.
Suddenly, another clone appears out of the wall, forcing Tanjiro to duck away and avoid it. When another appears behind him, Tanjiro tries to use his Water Breathing but is unable to react in time. As the demon gets close, it is kicked in the head by Nezuko emerging from her box. As Kazumi and the Swamp Demon watch with surprise, the demon questions why one of his kind is accompanying a swordsman.
Nezuko envisioning Takeo and Hanako.
Nezuko walks to Kazumi and the girl and envisions her siblings Takeo and Hanako in them. As Tanjiro see his sister's behavior, he remembers that Sakonji had informed him about something regarding Nezuko. As she slept, he tried to hypnotize her with a message: "All humans are your family. Protect humanity. Demons are your enemy. Never forgive demons for the harm they do".  Tanjiro watches as Nezuko prepares to battle the Swamp Demon, an angered expression written on her face.
Nezuko raises her leg and attempts to deliver an axe kick to the demon's clone, but it hides back into its swamp before she makes contact. Tanjiro warns her away from chasing after it and calls her to come back; as she does, another clone tries to grab her but she leaps over it and stands beside her brother. Remembering Sakonji's words that as a demon, Nezuko is no longer weak, Tanjiro wonders if he can leave Nezuko to protect Kazumi and the girl.
Tanjiro inside the demon's swamp.
Suddenly, the swamp puddle appears beneath him and he begins to sink in, but not before telling Nezuko to protect the two bystanders. Inside the murky lair, he sees a large number of clothes and belongings once owned by the demon's victims, calling his actions unforgivable. Two clones then appear and mock him for deciding to enter their domain, as there is almost no air and the heaviness of the swamp will slow him movement. Nonetheless, Tanjiro warns them not to doubt him, as the training he received on Mount Sagiri had made him accustomed to even thinner air than the swamp.
He then sees an opportunity to use a form that will best utilize his conditions underwater. The clones then swim around him at great speeds and at sharp angles, momentarily confusing him. However, he remains focused and knows he can kill them up close. He aligns his sword for a form made with unsteady footwork and able to generate a strong spin. As the clones get close, Tanjiro detects the Opening Thread and uses Water Breathing, Sixth Form: Whirlpool and slashes the two demons' necks at once with a powerful cutting vortex, killing them. Afterwards, he begins to feel the strain of the lack of air and swims to the surface to Nezuko.
Nezuko battles the last clone.
Above ground, Nezuko battles the last clone and lands a strong punch onto its stomach. It notes her strength without possessing any strange abilities and believes that she must have received much blood from Tanjiro. Nezuko is preventing him from entering his swamp, but the clone notes that her attacks are simple and easy to get accustomed to, as well as the futility of her attacks due to his healing. The clone succeeds in cutting Nezuko's face with his hand and dazes her. Seeing her standing still, he tries to kill her but has his right arm suddenly sliced off.
Tanjiro appears between them and cuts off its other limb. Falling to the ground and confronted by the Demon Slayer, the clone realizes that his other two selves have already been killed. Tanjiro admonishes them for their number of victims and the demon only growls at him that when women age, they get ugly and taste bad. When it claims the victims should be thankful they were devoured, Tanjiro angrily slashes its mouth to prevent it from talking further. Pointing his blade at the demon, he demands it tell him everything he knows about Muzan Kibutsuji. To his surprise, the demon suddenly becomes frightened.
Muzan threatens the Swamp Demon.
The demon remembers when Muzan Kibutsuji had threatened him severely. Grabbed by the neck and lifted up, he hears Muzan's threats to never say his name to anyone, as he will immediately know and that he will always be watching him.
Despite being threatened with death, the terrified demon denies Tanjiro's question about Muzan and shakes his head, incessantly rambling that he cannot say anything. Watching the demon tremble uncontrollably, he notes the strong scent of fear in him. Growing back his arms instantly, the demon yells out that he cannot say anything and tries to attack Tanjiro, forcing him to cut through his neck, killing the demon once and for all. Once more, Tanjiro is dismayed that he has not gotten any information.
Tanjiro returns to find a sleeping Nezuko and apologizes to her once again for failing to gather intel on how to revert her back into a human. He sees Kazumi on the floor with a distraught look on his face and checks to see if he is alright. Kazumi rhetorically asks him if he looks alright after having lost the love of his life, to which Tanjiro advises him to keep living no matter how many times he might lose something precious to him. Angered by his dismissive demeanor, Kazumi belittles Tanjiro, asking what he would know about losing something precious being just a child.
Tanjiro smiles at Kazumi.
Tanjiro gives him a gentle smile and offers Kazumi the hair bow that belonged to Satoko, to give him something to remember her by. Realizing his insensitive mistake, Kazumi apologizes to Tanjiro as he leaves the village, sadly looking at his callused hand and knowing it was only possible through relentless training. As he makes his exit from the village, Tanjiro makes the realization that he is not the only one to suffer loss from demons, blaming Muzan for all the pain they have caused. His Kasugai Crow then lands on his shoulder and immediately informs him to investigate a rumor regarding a hidden demon in Asakusa, dismaying Tanjiro that he already has a new mission immediately after his last.
Two days after leaving the village, Tanjiro and Nezuko arrive in the bustling city of Asakusa. Being raised in the mountains the majority of his life, he are immediately overwhelmed by the enormous crowds, large buildings, and stunning lights. They take a break from the crowds and arrive at a noodle cart at the city's edge where Nezuko sleeps and Tanjiro grabs a bite to eat. However as he awaits for his meal, he is caught off guard by an unexpected familiar scent nearby.
Tanjiro meets Muzan Kibutsuji in Asakusa.
He takes off following the trail and discovers Muzan Kibutsuji hidden within the crowds of people. He reaches for his katana and is about to engage Muzan before he realizes that he is carrying a young child in his arms. Muzan is joined shortly after by his wife. He stands before him horrified and confused as to why the young girl and her mother are with him. The young woman then goes on to ask Muzan if he has any sort of affiliation with Tanjiro, to which he denies.
While the woman and the young child look at Tanjiro, Muzan reaches behind and quickly scratches the neck of a pedestrian, turning him into a demon. The only one to witness this, Tanjiro reaches forward to try and subdue the newly transformed demon before he attacks anyone, but fails as the man begins attacking his wife.

Tanjiro tries to stop the new demon.
The newly transformed demon bites into his wife's shoulder, horrifying the crowd around them. Tanjiro runs at the demon and pulls him away from her, stuffing his hood into his mouth as a muzzle. Despite her concerns for him, Tanjiro orders her to put pressure on her bite. Muzan tells his frightened wife that it would be best to move away and they leave the situation.
Seeing his target escaping, Tanjiro yells out Muzan's name and declares he will never let him get away. His wife becomes worried at his behavior but Muzan instead notices Tanjiro's earrings. As he declares that he will feel his sword on his neck, proclaiming he would never forgive him, the demon remembers when a Demon Slayer had him cornered, and that he too was wearing Tanjiro's earrings.
The authorities arrive at the scene and order Tanjiro to release the man immediately, not knowing his demonic nature. Tanjiro pleads with them to either restrain the man or to not interfere, not wanting any harm to come to anyone else. The police ignore him and try to pull the boy off but Tanjiro desperately holds on, unwilling to let the demon go.
Two demons offer help to Tanjiro.
A woman is seen engraving her nails into her arms causing her wounds to bleed. Tanjiro notices a shift in the scent of the environment and an illusionary pattern engulfs his vision. The police are blinded by the patterns and can no longer see Tanjiro. He goes on the defensive thinking that he is about to get attacked by another demon but is surprised when the woman comes forward accompanied by a boy. She reveals that she is as he had detected, a demon, and adds her intentions of wanting to help Tanjiro defeat Muzan.
Elsewhere in Asakusa, Muzan claims to his wife and daughter that he has a meeting to attend to, and adds that he will ask the police about the "incident" earlier, easing his family's concern. As they ride away in a taxi, Muzan shortcuts through an alleyway but accidentally bumps a drunk man. He apologizes and walks away but the man holds onto him. Muzan again apologizes and claims he is in a hurry but the drunkard does not take kindly to Muzan's expensive clothes, before mocking his skin complexion and claiming he looks half-dead.
Enraged, Muzan immediately kills the man with one swing of his arm and his lifeless body is slammed head first against a wall. The second larger man angrily approaches Muzan and demands an explanation for what happened to the other man, who he regards as his brother, and the woman accompanying the men cries out as she realizes he is dead. To her horror, she looks back to see that Muzan has killed the second man by kicking him in the air with such force that blood spews out from his mouth and rains down on her below.
Muzan finally approaches the terrified woman and mocks her with a series of questions regarding his appearance. He touches her forehead and forcefully pierces her skull, injecting massive amounts of his blood into her, as he tells her that she will not be able to withstand the transformation and her cells will disintegrate one by one. The woman starts to scream but quickly transforms into a demon-like creature before dissolving into ash.
At the snap of his fingers, two new individuals appear before Muzan, with him instructing them to kill the "demon hunter with the hanafuda earrings", alluding to Tanjiro.
At the udon vendor from earlier, the owner yells at Nezuko for not eating his food. She sits there puzzled by his anger until Tanjiro returns and takes the chopsticks from the vendors hands and quickly slurps down the noodles. He thanks and compliments the vendor's cooking before leaving with Nezuko, and the man is left somewhat angry but still flattered by his compliment.
As they walk down the street, Tanjiro apologizes for leaving Nezuko alone but is suddenly stopped by her wariness of someone at the end of the street. Tanjiro calls out him who turns out to be the demon from earlier, letting him know that there was no need to wait for him as he could've followed the scent back to the hideout. The demon rejects his claim saying that there was no way that they could be tracked and questions Nezuko's presence -since she's a demon- while simultaneously calling her a hag. Tanjiro is insulted by his remark and argues that his sister is in fact considered his town's beauty.
Nezuko and an annoyed Tanjiro following the demon.
They travel behind the demon until they arrive at a house with a pinned piece of paper. When they enter the building they stumble upon the demon lady treating the injured woman who was attacked by her spouse. Out of curiosity, Tanjiro questions if it is hard for the woman to resist wanting to attack the humans that she treats. Before she is able to respond, the demon beside him elbows Tanjiro and berates him for asking such a ridiculous question. The woman chides her assistant to stop being violent and formally introduces themselves as Tamayo and Yushiro.
Going back to Tanjiro's question, she explains that she is different from normal demons since she has altered her body and removed Muzan's curse. She goes into detail saying that she doesn't need to feed on human flesh, and only needs to drink small amounts of human blood in order to survive. Her methods involve purchasing blood from poor individuals under the facade that they would be used for medical transfusions, explaining why they do not have a distinct demon scent. Tamayo reveals that Yushiro requires less blood then she does and that he was the only individual that she was able to successfully transform into a demon after experimenting for more than 200 years.
Tanjiro and Nezuko meeting Tamayo at her office.
Being stunned by her claims, Tanjiro brazenly asks Tamayo how old she truly is, causing Yushiro to hit him in a rage. She sternly warn him not to hit Tanjiro again, before then explaining that she does not have ill intentions to increase the number of demons in the world; she simply strives to find a solution to treat the incurable so they can live a little longer. Tanjiro senses her pure intent and decides to seek Tamayo's help in finding a way to turn demons back into humans.
In an alley at another part of the city, walking down the street, a demon playing with a temari ball is seen accompanying a second demon with eyes on his hands, who begins to track a set footprints on the floor. The Arrow Demon accurately identifies their provided targets, and when the Temari Demon asks how they will kill them, he answer they will do so brutally.
Tamayo reprimanding Yushiro for hitting Tanjiro
Tamayo confirms Tanjiro's suspicions on being able to turn a demon back into a human. He rushes forward to Tamayo eager to know the method but Yushiro flips him back, preventing him from getting too close to Tamayo. She angrily warns Yushiro again not to hit Tanjiro to which he cheekily responds, "I just threw him. I did not hit him". Tamayo tells Tanjiro that in order to establish a cure, she would need to study Nezuko's blood and that he would need to collect samples from demon who contain high concentrations of Muzan's blood. She goes on to inform him that Nezuko has a rare and special condition regarding the fact that she had slept for two years to regain her strength and since she hasn't consumed human or animal flesh within that period.
Tamayo warns Tanjiro that the task of collecting demon blood would not be easy and questions if he would still be willing to try. Tanjiro responds, " If that's the only way, I'll do it. It will help, not just Nezuko but lots of others right?", and a relieved Tamayo smiles at his optimism; Tanjiro blushes slightly at her smile but quickly realizes that Yushiro is displeased. At that moment, a speeding temari begin to destroy the house's interior.
Having battered the interior and exterior of the house, the Temari Demon is impressed that her accomplice Yahaba had detected it, since it was hidden by a Blood Demon Art. He calls on her to see if their chosen target is inside but additionally chides the demon, Susamaru, for dirtying his kimono with her messy way of attacking. Bemused, she tells him to stop complaining about his clothes as she has found the inhabitants with her attack.
Hunching over Nezuko to protect her, Tanjiro is shocked to discover all the damage done was through hurling a simple temari. Yushiro sees her and wonders if the demon is a servant of Muzan. Susamaru throws her weapon again and it bounces inside the house, forcing everyone to duck. When Yushiro stands up to face her, he is suddenly decapitated when the temari unexpectedly swerves into his head. In disbelief at seeing him take a hit, Tanjiro orders Nezuko to take the injured woman away to safety.
As Susamaru laughs over killing one of her opponents, Tanjiro points his blade at the demon and notes that her scent is far stronger than all of the demons he had previously battle. Suddenly, she remarks that "the Demon Slayer with hanafuda earrings... is you", causing him to realize he is her target. He tells Tamayo to fall back, and she responds that he mustn't worry about them since they can heal. Susamaru then hurls a temari right at him; utilizing his fastest form, Tanjiro stabs it dead-on with Water Breathing, Seventh Form: Drop Ripple Thrust - Curve.
Susamaru gets serious.
Only mildly surprised, Susamaru seemingly causes the temari to slide of his blade and come back to her, with Tanjiro noting its unnatural movement were also evident when it struck Yushiro. Tamayo holds Yushiro's body and sees his neck and mouth heal, speaking of his dismay in Tamayo becoming associated with Tanjiro, since his concealment-based Blood Demon Art cannot fully hide something's existence. Healing the rest of his head, he declares his hatred of anyone interfering with his time with her.
Laughing at Yushiro's threats, Susamaru removes her kimono and states that they should be honored to be killed by her, a member of the Twelve Kizuki. She grows two new pairs of arms and creates four more temaris, now totalling six. Hurling them all at once, she succeeds in injuring both Yushiro and Tamayo, while Tanjiro struggles to find a way to stop them. Yushiro chastises him for not see the arrows; when Tanjiro becomes confused, the demon attaches a talisman imbued with his sight to his head, giving him the ability to see that the temaris being led by invisible arrows.
Nezuko attacks a hiding Yahaba.
Now able to see their direction, he directs Nezuko's attention to up a tree in the backyard, where Yahaba is hiding and controlling them. Nezuko repeatedly kicks him, causing the arrows to weaken when Susamaru throws them at Tanjiro, and he quickly uses the Water Breathing, Third Form: Flowing Dance to cut through them all.
He then rushes the Temari Demon and cuts off all her arms at once. Asking Tamayo if the demons are close to Muzan, she answers that they may be, giving him the motivation to give her their blood.
Yushiro reminds Tanjiro to stay vigilant as if the demons truly are two of the Twelve Kizuki, they will be stronger than any he has previously faced. As Tanjiro acknowledges his warning, he then suggests to Tamayo that they should run while the enemy is distracted with Tanjiro and Nezuko. When she gives him a horrified look, he quickly says he was "just joking."
Yushiro ordering Tanjiro to battle Yahaba first while he and Tamayo will work with Nezuko to handle Susamaru
At the same time, Nezuko has gone after Yahaba, kicking him repeatedly to force him out of the tree. Annoyed by the dust being kicked up, he telekinetically pushes the demon away from him. Susamaru quickly heals all of her arms, which Tanjiro notes is faster than any demon from Final Selection had managed to do, before colliding with Nezuko being shoved by Yahaba.  Yushiro orders Tanjiro to battle Yahaba first while he and Tamayo will work with Nezuko to handle Susamaru. Before continuing on to Yahaba, Tanjiro tells Nezuko to be careful and the girl then briefly sees Tamayo and Yushiro as her mother and Rokuta, giving her the determination to protect them.
Tanjiro and Nezuko switch targets.
The siblings switch positions and go after their respective targets. Facing off with Yahaba, Tanjiro sees the Opening Thread, but it very quickly snaps when Yahaba tells Tanjiro to stay away from him, using arrows to disrupt his footwork. The arrows continue to drag him around the yard before throwing him high into the air. The demon then withholds the arrow's pull, causing the Demon Slayer to plummet, only surviving by using Water Breathing, Eighth Form: Waterfall Basin to break his fall.
Tamayo warning Nezuko not to kick the temari.
Yahaba then notes to Susamaru that Tamayo is a runaway demon and believes she would make a good present for Muzan. Susamaru agrees and hurls a temari straight to Nezuko. Though Tamayo warns her not to kick it, Nezuko makes contact and the temari breaks off her right foot. As she is down, Susamaru kicks her into the house where she slams into the wall. The Temari Demon wonders if all four would be good enough to kill, though the Arrow Demon only sees value in Tanjiro and Tamayo.
Inside the house, Tamayo gives Nezuko a serum to accelerate her slow regeneration. Tanjiro meanwhile is unable to find a way to bypass the arrows, seeing as they are moving too fast, he cannot cut them with his sword, and because they will disrupt any chance he makes at attacking Yahaba. An arrow then twirls around his arm, Yahaba intending to twist it off; Tanjiro quickly leaps upwards, causing his body to spin and keep his arm in motion, breaking free and annoying the demon.
Thinking quickly, he surmises that he can use multiple forms together and change the arrows' direction. As Yahaba sends them to kill Tanjiro, he uses Water Breathing, Sixth Form: Whirlpool: Flow and catches them all in his sword's direction. Despite the heavy weight of his blade, Tanjiro musters the strength to use Second Form: Lateral Water Wheel, Improved, successfully beheading Yahaba.
Tanjiro caught in Yahaba's arrows.
After successfully decapitating Yahaba, Tanjiro notes that the Whirlpool form, though weaker in open air, was able to gain momentum by using the arrows. Yahaba rants and curses the Demon Slayer for ruining his chance at recognition from Muzan, declaring he would never forgive him. Suddenly numerous arrows begin to form within Tanjiro, the Arrow Demon intending to kill him as he dies.
Suddenly pulled, Tanjiro becomes alarmed and uses the Water Breathing, Fourth Form: Striking Tide to avoid crashing into a wall. The arrows start throwing his body in multiple directions and he is forced to use continuous breathing techniques such as the Water Breathing, Second Form: Water Wheel, then Drop Ripple Thrust, Water Surface Slash, Waterfall Basin, Water Wheel and then Striking Tide, to protect himself; while doing so, he notes that he had never used so many forms at once. Eventually, the arrows fade and Tanjiro is released.
He manages to land back to the ground with the Water Breathing, Sixth Form: Whirlpool. However, his body has already sustained a substantial amount of damage, leaving him with a broken leg and multiple rib fractures. Tanjiro lays on the ground, wincing from the pain but nonetheless grabs hold of his blade in his mouth and wills himself to move. He proceeds to crawl on the floor towards everyone else, mentally pleading for Tamayo, Yushiro, and Nezuko to be safe.
At the same time, Susamaru suddenly sees her own temari launched at her by Nezuko. Having healed and kicked it back the Temari Demon, Nezuko then engages her in a back and forth confrontation, kicking a temari at each other with increasing power and speed. Eventually, Nezuko is able to absorb the momentum and kick it back with such force, even Susamaru is forced to dodge it. Yushiro wonders if the drug Tamayo had given her had also improved her strength, but she notes that all it did was aid her regeneration.
Susamaru is affected by Muzan's curse.
They are witnessing Nezuko's own strength without devouring humans. Despite this, Tamayo knows that should Susamaru utilize her full strength, even Nezuko would lose.  As Susamaru begins to feel excitement over seeing Nezuko's power, Tamayo stands in front of Nezuko and asks the Temari Demon of what she knows of Muzan. Susamaru attempts to dismiss her as the runaway unworthy of speaking about him but Tamayo claims that Muzan is little more than a coward who is always afraid.
Angered, Susamaru tries to silence her but Tamayo continues, saying the true reasons demons don't group up isn't because they will eat each other but because Muzan fears they will all overpower his control.  Aghast, Susamaru attempts to defend her master's honour, speaking about his unmatched strength and abilities. Yushiro notes that Tamayo has used an ability. Suddenly, the Temari Demon, in her defence of Muzan, says his last name, horrifying her.
Tamayo had used Magical Aroma of Daylight: a truth serum-like spell that inhibits brain function on the affected and prevents them from withholding secrets. Tamayo mentions that saying his name will trigger the curse, and though she pities her, she had no choice. Now frightened, Susamaru runs away and desperately begs for Muzan's forgiveness, only for her body to drastically change, hunching over in pain. As Tanjiro watches, three giant arms burst from the Temari Demon's body.
Yushiro covering Tanjiro's face with a cloth
Susamaru's body is torn apart by the arms summoned by Muzan's curse. The gory scene leaves everyone in a state of shock as her body is dismantled. In the aftermath, Tanjiro asks Tamayo if Susamaru was dead and she responds that she will be shortly. She describes how fighting between demons is pointless as sunlight and beheading through Nichirin Swords are the only two ways to cause major damage; however, Muzan alone appears to be capable of destroying demons. Yushiro approaches Tanjiro and covers his face with a cloth, preventing him from breathing in Tamayo's Blood Demon Art since it is harmful to humans.
Tamayo looks at Susamaru's eyeball and reports that she was not one of the Twelve Kizuki, much to Tanjiro's dismay. She mentions how a true member would have a number engraved on their eyeball, but Susamaru and Yahaba do not, as they are too weak. Tanjiro is shocked to learn this since they put up a difficult fight. She nonetheless collects blood from Susamaru's corpse and apologizes to Tanjiro for letting Nezuko breathe in some of her spell, moving to examine her. Yushiro remarks that the demons deserved their fate for threatening Tamayo, before leaving Tanjiro to hold the cloth by himself.
Tanjiro recovers Susamaru's temari ball.
While he tries to pick himself up, Tanjiro hears a voice from Susamaru's remains asking for her temari. Slowly, he picks up the last remaining temari and places it next to her remains, listening to her asking for someone to "play" with. He notes that despite the number of people she had killed, she still retained a childish personality. As the sun comes up and her corpse completely disintegrates, Tanjiro finds no justice in her fate, being manipulated, forced to fight, and eventually killed by the one whom she worshipped. He pins the blame on Muzan and deems him a "true demon".
Tanjiro moves back into the house, going to the basement where the three demons are sheltering. Nezuko runs over to give him a hug, then runs back to Tamayo to also hug her and pat Yushiro on the head, much to Yushiro's annoyance. Confused, Tamayo questions Tanjiro for Nezuko's actions and he replies that she likely thought of them as her family, treating them as the humans she must protect rather than demons. He expresses relief that Nezuko still maintains her own will until Tamayo starts crying, shocking Tanjiro. He asks Nezuko to stop hugging her as it was rude and profusely apologizes to Tamayo, but she thanks her instead and pulls Nezuko closer.
Nezuko hugs Tamayo, much to Yushiro's jealousy.
Seeing her vulnerable, Yushiro remembers the day he had first met Tamayo: dying to a terminal illness. Tamayo then explains that thought their professions as doctors allows them to stay hidden, eventually, they will be discovered as demons and asks Tanjiro if he would allow Nezuko to stay with them as it was much safer than on the battlefield, much to Yushiro's displeasure. He ponders for a bit but Nezuko grabs his hand and knowingly looks at him. Tanjiro smiles and thanks Tamayo for the offer, but he preferred to be by Nezuko's side at all times, never again being separated and thinks of his family. Tamayo accepts his choice, wishing him good luck and bids farewell. Before the siblings leave, Yushiro concedes his earlier statement and calls Nezuko beautiful, much to Tanjiro's pleasure.
Later during that day, Tanjiro's Kasugai Crow continually harasses him to go to south-southeast. While requesting for his crow to be more quiet, the two suddenly hear a loud voice coming from a yellow haired boy, seen on the road begging a girl to marry him.

Tanjiro stops Zenitsu.
The sparrow of the yellow-haired Demon Slayer begs for Tanjiro's help. He grabs him and pulls him away from the girl, asking if he cannot see she wants nothing to do with him. Suddenly, the boy notices that Tanjiro is also wearing a Demon Slayer Corps uniform. Tanjiro denies knowing him but the stranger remembers him from Final Selection.
Tanjiro pulling a girl off Zenitsu.
Tanjiro ignores him and tells the girl he was harassing that it was alright for her to return home, and she thanks him. Panicking, he yells that she couldn't leave as she "liked" him and they had to be married. He is responded to with a slap from her, and she starts beating him, prompting Tanjiro to hurry over and pull her off, asking her to calm down. She berates the stranger, stating that she never liked him and only talked to him because she thought he was wounded or sick when he lied on the side of the road. Shocked, he replies that he thought she was helping him out of love and worry. The girl angrily mentions it was impossible as she has a fiancé, stomping away and telling him he appeared fine now and hoped they would never met again.
Tanjiro chiding Zenitsu for his lack of shame.
Heartbroken, the Demon Slayer complains to Tanjiro about his interference, in which he receives a disgusted face as a reply. He demands him to not use that face as it looked like he was looking at him as some sort of creature, before blaming him for preventing his "marriage." Again, Tanjiro only replies with the same face, much to his annoyance. He claims that he is about to die as he was weak, begging Tanjiro to protect him before he got married. Tanjiro doesn't respond and introduces himself, to which the Demon Slayer introduces himself as Zenitsu Agatsuma. Tanjiro starts chiding Zenitsu for his lack of shame, in which he replies that he was deceived by a woman and indebted, saved by his master but forced to train harshly every day, sorrowfully stating his dislike for his occupation. Tanjiro gives him his lunch and tells him he understands, but he should cause less trouble for his sparrow.
Tanjiro and Zenitsu arrive at the Tsuzumi Mansion.
Both Demon Slayers arrive at Tanjiro's assigned mission, a mansion in a mountain forest. Tanjiro smells blood from inside and Zenitsu hears an unusual sound, before they see two children huddled together at the edge of the forest. They try to approach them, but the children move away in fright. Noticing the fact that they were likely still in shock from something, Tanjiro entertains them with Zenitsu's sparrow, calming them down. The older child, tells Tanjiro that their older brother was kidnapped when they were walking in the night, and the kidnapper went into the house. Tanjiro praises him and his sister for following the monster, but the boy cries and said they followed his blood trail, upset that their older brother was hurt. Tanjiro soothes them and said he would defeat the monster and save their brother, much to their relief.
Zenitsu asking if Tanjiro can hear something.
Zenitsu suddenly retorts hearing a sound similar to a drum, expressing discomfort. Tanjiro replies that he couldn't hear a sound but is interrupted by a man flying out of the window, falling onto the ground. Tanjiro rushes over to check on him, alarmed at his deep wound. The man says he finally got out and asks if he was going to die, in which Tanjiro can only respond to with a hug. All of a sudden, a large sound comes out of the house, coming from a strange demon.
Tanjiro giving Zenitsu a spiteful look.
Tanjiro distraughtly realizes the man that fell out of the house is now dead, upset at the amount of pain he must've felt. The older child tells him their brother was wearing a persimmon-colored kimino and the man that had just perished was not him. Tanjiro internally apologizes to the deceased man, promising to give him a burial when he returns. He calls for Zenitsu to join him on the mission to defeat the demon in the house, but after looking at Zenitsu's distressed face, angrily goes on alone. Scared by Tanjiro's furious expression, Zenitsu reluctantly tags along. Before they enter the house, Tanjiro entrusts Nezuko's box to the two children, telling them that what's in the box will protect them in case of danger.
Tanjiro enters the Tsuzumi Mansion.
As the two Demon Slayers enter the house, Zenitsu trembles and confides in Tanjiro to protect him. He apologizes to him, saying he has multiple broken bones and Zenitsu cries in shock, protesting that he was no longer safe without someone to protect him despite Tanjiro's attempts to comfort him. Unexpectedly, the children run inside the house, frightened by the noises coming out of Tanjiro's box and a dismayed Tanjiro tells them they couldn't just leave it outside as it was more important than his life.
The group Tanjiro, Zenitsu, Teruko, and Shoichi accidentally get accidentally gets separated from each other.
Suddenly, the group hears a sound and accidentally gets separated , Zenitsu with the boy and Tanjiro with the girl. The latter pair is stunned to see the room change, with Tanjiro noticing how it shifted with a drum's beat. He apologizes to her for separating from her brother and vows to protect her, wiping her tears. Asking for her name, she answers she is Teruko. They hear footsteps and are shocked by the sudden presence of a giant demon in the hallway. Tanjiro immediately deciphers him to be the master of the house; his scent was the strongest and covered a broad range of the building.
Somewhere else, Zenitsu wails about his certain death while the boy, Shoichi, simultaneously calls out for Teruko. Zenitsu pulls Shoichi and tells him they should go outside, but Shoichi turns around and reprimands him for his cowardice. Zenitsu is hurt by his words and argues that children should not be involved in this situation. They make their way down the hall and through doors, but fail to find the entrance. Opening a particular set of doors, Zenitsu comes face-to-face with an individual wearing a boar hide mask. Zenitsu calls him a monster, and the individual runs out of the room and rushes through a hallway.
A Demon Slayer with a boar mask crashes through.
Elsewhere, Tanjiro covers Teruko's mouth, informing her not to scream and to hide behind the shelves. The demon then speaks, annoyed at the number of people barging into his home and ranting about "my prey". Tanjiro faces the demon head-on, introduces himself as a Demon Slayer and the one that will defeat him. It ignores him and mutters about found children with "marechi" as Tanjiro goes to attack. However, the demon suddenly beats a drum and the entire room rotates, Tanjiro speculating the change to be a result of the demon's Blood Demon Art. He senses a new smell and the boar-masked individual crashes through the wall.
Tanjiro is astonished by the presence of the masked stranger. He notices the individual wields two Nichirin Swords and witnesses his assertion of using the Drum Demon as his stepping stone to become stronger and higher-ranked, rushing forward to attack him. The demon beats its drum and the room rotates with Tanjiro yelling at Teruko to grab hold of furniture as she tumbles. The dual-wielder uses Tanjiro as a support to launch off and attack the demon as Tanjiro tells him to not act recklessly.
The stranger tramples Teruko.
He is ignored and the Drum Demon hits another drum, shifting the room which results in the boar-masked individual landing and stepping on Teruko, paying no mind to her cries and expressing enjoyment and interest in the motion of the room. Tanjiro throws the stranger off of her and hugs Teruko, angry over his lack of concern for a little girl's well-being. The masked Demon Slayer laughs and begins attacking him, praising Tanjiro for being capable of throwing him. Tanjiro shouts at him to stop as the demon is right in front of them, but he states that he didn't care and continues his assault.
Tanjiro and the stranger evade Kyogai's three slashes.
The Drum Demon suddenly hits a different drum, resulting in three quick slashes cutting the floor and interrupting the scuffle between the two Demon Slayers. Tanjiro comments on the shape of the slashes looking like claw marks, but his thoughts are cut off by the demon consecutively hitting multiple drums and rotating the room once again. He starts understanding how the movement corresponds to each drum that is hit, but he and Teruko are transported to another room before he can react.
Kiyoshi uses the tsuzumi.
Tanjiro questions the sudden change, as he didn't hear Kyogai hit a drum which could've possibly allowed for him and Teruko to move. He starts analyzing his surroundings and finds a dead body, in which the Demon Slayer quickly ushers Teruko in the other direction before she sees it. Tanjiro then smells a unique scent of blood and he opens a set of door, discovering the siblings' oldest brother Kiyoshi right before he hits a drum.
In another section of the house, Zenitsu walks while holding Shoichi's hand. Shoichi says his name and Zenitsu yells, scolding him for surprising him. The boy tells the Demon Slayer how he feels unsafe around him, especially considering how frightened Zenitsu was. He profusely apologizes and tells him that they should stay quiet to avoid being attacked by demons, just as one crawls from under the mansion's foundations and appears in front of them.
Zenitsu begging for Shoichi to run away.
Zenitsu immediately yells at the appearance of the demon, desperately telling it to stay back and that neither he nor Shoichi would taste good as they run away. It responds that he would not know how they'd taste if he didn't try, proceeding to chase and attack them. As they turn into a room, the demon tries to use its long tongue to grab them, missing and hitting a pot instead. With the room being a dead end and their exit blocked, Zenitsu begins begging for Shoichi to run away, though the boy does not deem it a wise decision. The Demon Slayer berates himself for being a coward and tries to find the courage to help save Shoichi.
As the demon enters the room, it threatens to devour his brain through his ear. This finally causes Zenitsu to become overwhelmed with fear and lose consciousness. As he slumps to the ground, Shoichi shakes him to get his attention but is shocked to see him genuinely asleep. The demon becomes confused seeing the unusual situation but does not dwell further, extending its tongue to grab Shoichi.
Zenitsu kills the Tongue Demon.
Suddenly, the demon's tongue is cut and Zenitsu stands up. As Shoichi and the demon watch in confusion, Zenitsu bows down and begins to breathe. He uses the Thunder Breathing, First Form: Thunderclap and Flash to decapitate the demon in an instant. Shoichi gapes in shock as Zenitsu quickly wakes up and screams at the sight of the dead demon's head rolling next to him. The confused Demon Slayer misunderstands the situation and expresses extreme gratitude towards Shoichi for "saving" the pair, telling him he should've let him know earlier that he was so strong. The boy is at a loss for words and decides not to say anything, telling Zenitsu they should go on.
The Horned Demon discovers the stranger.
In a hallway of the house, the boar-masked Demon Slayer runs through, annoyed by the Drum Demon blowing him away despite his attempt to hunt it down and the inconvenience of the hallway's structure.
