Doma believes he was born to make it his duty to make these people happy, by devouring them whole.
After a fifth stab on his hand fails to hurt him, Doma quickly heals himself of Shinobu's poison, before asking if she is okay after noticing she is breathing heavily. Shinobu realizes the true strength of an Upper Rank, noting Doma's resistance and the inability of her poisons to work on him. He tells her that her lungs' cells are dying after accidentally inhaling his Blood Demon Art, now making it dangerous to breathe. She then decides to use multiple blows to poison him with a larger dosage.
Doma slashes Shinobu as she retreats.
Shinobu uses Insect Breathing, Dance of the Dragonfly: Compound Eye Hexagon and rushes forward, stabbing Doma six times. He remarks that the Insect Hashira might be the fastest one he has fought, but as she backs away, Shinobu bleeds profusely, realizes she herself was also slashed in return before she could notice. Doma taunts her as she collapses to the floor in pain, mentioning that she could have easily cut off his head with her immense speed but can't due to her small frame. As blood falls on her hands, she sees just how small they are.
She remembers that she never grew taller, lamenting that she could have killed demons the usual way had she grown a bit more. Shinobu knows larger hands and legs meant more muscle and that it was a distinct advantage. She recalls that Kanae too was of a dainty frame despite being taller than her, and remarks that Gyomei has it easy with his strength, putting others at ease when he fight. Shinobu remembers Kanae's last moments with her, telling her that she would likely lose to Doma too.
Kanae's spirit appears before the injured Shinobu, telling her to stand. Shinobu believes she no longer can after losing so much blood, and with her left lung damaged by Doma's attack, she cannot breathe normally as well. Kanae declares this irrelevant and states she will win with the right resolve to kill him no matter the sacrifice, noting that she promised to her and to Kanao. Remembering their younger sister, Shinobu crouches down while Doma approaches her, noting the slashes he gave was only half-hearted, making it very painful for her. Kanae urges her younger sister to keep trying, causing her to stand up and surprising the Upper Rank. As she stares at Doma, Shinobu starts to cough blood, prompting Doma to laugh that the blood in her lungs is causing her to do so.
Shinobu evades Doma's slash and stabs him in the neck.
Resolving to behead Shinobu to end her pain, he tells her to give up, claiming she is already beyond saving. Instead, Shinobu makes a last stand, and using Insect Breathing, Dance of the Centipede: Hundred-Legged Zigzag, she speeds towards the Upper Rank to attack him. Doma is shocked at this feat, noting the destroyed bridge from the impact of her feet; he tries to slash her in response but is unable to make contact, only managing to slice her haori. Shinobu crouches down and launches into the air, driving her sword through Doma's neck and forcing his body into the ceiling in one final thrust.
Shinobu and Kanae's parents are killed.
Shinobu remembers her childhood, once believing that happiness was an endless road throughout life. That belief was shattered when a demon entered her home and killed both her parents, leaving her and Kanae orphaned. They were saved however by Gyomei Himejima, who had arrived and quickly defeated the demon. Shinobu realized that though her happiness was forever destroyed, other people's weren't, and the sisters resolved to defeat demons and prevent others from suffering the same fate as them.
She and Kanae made a promise to each other to both be Demon Slayers to do so. The two believed that despite their weak strength, stopping one demon could save dozens of people, and stopping an Upper Rank could save hundreds. It wasn't a matter of whether they could or could not, because some things in life necessitated doing.
Recalling the time when Tanjiro had asked if she was angry, she states she has been so for a long time, remembering her parents' death, her sister's death, and the deaths of all her Tsugukos before Kanao. She remembers Aoi, Sumi, Kiyo and Naho, how their families too were killed. Most of all, she is incensed at her poison's inability to hurt Doma. Her swords slips from Doma's neck, causing her to fall, but he uses his ice to catch her and pulls Shinobu into a hug.
Doma pulling Shinobu into a hug.
Doma commends Shinobu for her admirable efforts, impressed that a weak girl could do so much. Though she is not talented like Kanae, she has done well as a Demon Slayer and calls it miraculous that she isn't dead yet. It was futile to kill him, and yet she was foolish enough to try anyways, calling her fruitless endeavour the folly and wonder of humanity. Declaring that she is now worthy to be eaten and they can live together forever, Doma asks for the Insect Hashira's last words; Shinobu bitterly tells him, "Go to Hell!"
Doma absorbs Shinobu's body.
Kanao opens the door to the cult room and looks up to see Doma clutching her in the roof. Shinobu attempts to signal Kanao with her hand, but Doma notices it. As she watches, Doma breaks Shinobu's body in his arms, to Kanao's horror, killing her and causing her sword to fall from her hand. She desperately leaps upwards to use Flower Breathing, Fourth Form: Crimson Hanagoromo but misses when Doma escapes and lands onto the floor. The demon advises her not to attack him in the middle of absorbing someone, causing Kanao to seethe with rage.
Doma fails to taunt her into fighting him, wondering if Shinobu had signalled with her hands. He asks if Kanao was told about his powers, impressed that Shinobu only conveyed it in a moment. As he pats her disappearing head, the demon notes that the Hashira tried her best despite it being futile; he comments favourably about his night as "such fine feasts keep showing up one after another." As she stares at Upper Two, Kanao internalizes the feeling that somehow, the people she cares about will be alive tomorrow, and yet, it remains a fleeting hope that she cannot promise with certainty. "Why do people believe such things?"
Zenitsu approaches a room and calls for the individual inside to come out. They only respond that Zenitsu's beckoning is the improper address to a senior. Kaigaku walks out and taunts him for being as shabby as ever, but Zenitsu responds that seeing him now as a demon, he no longer recognizes Kaigaku as his senior.
As Tanjiro and Giyu run through the Infinity Castle, the former nearly falls through an opened floor, only barely managing to grab the ledge and save himself. As Giyu warns him to keep aware and alert, Tanjiro remarks it is as if the castle is alive, actively trying to separate him from Giyu. Knowing he must reach Muzan and the rest of the Corps' members, he then realizes Tamayo is running out of time, and yet they don't know where Muzan is.
A Kasugai crow then calls out the announcement that Shinobu is now dead, killed in a battle against Upper Rank Two. Upon hearing it, Tanjiro wells up with tears thinking about Kanao and the girls of the Butterfly Mansion. At the same time, Giyu notices the crow has a piece of paper attached to its neck, remarking that messages are being sent rather quickly.
Kiriya Ubuyashiki, the new Oyakata of the Demon Slayer Corps.
Similar pieces of paper, talismans of Yushiro's Blood Demon Art, appears on the head of Kiriya Ubuyashiki and his sister Kanata and Kuina. Kuina confirms Shinobu's death to Kiriya and notes the remaining Hashira are alive. He asks if she is the only one to have faced an Upper Rank and Kuina answers she is not; he then asks Kanata if all the crows sent with Yushiro's vision talismans have reached half of the Demon Slayers, to which she answers they have not.
Being the eldest son, Kiriya has now taken the mantle of Oyakata at the age of eight. Despite the deaths of his parents and sister, Kiriya does not mourn them and instead focuses on the mission, having no time to shed tears. Kuina and Kanata have also pushed their grief aside to help him. His deceased elder sisters were Nichika and Hinaki, who never left their parents' side.
As a father, Kagaya was strict in rearing his children due to his short life, quickly raising them into adulthood; Amane was similarly firm as well. With his death, Kiriya is now the leader of the Demon Slayer Corps. Due to their lacking information, Kiriya orders the crows to spread as many talismans as possible. Kuina confirms Muzan's location has not change and the Hashira are spread thin; he orders them to head north. Kuina adds that the two Demon Slayers currently facing Upper Ranks are Kanao and Zenitsu, who is facing Upper Rank Six.
Zenitsu informing Kaigaku of Jigoro's death.
Kaigaku claims that Zenitsu has not changed. "You're still a shabby, little runt. Still weak." He asks if he is now a Hashira and if he is still only able to use the first form. Zenitsu responds by noting Kaigaku's excitement in attaining the lowest position of the Upper Ranks, a rank he has taken that is only meant to fill a blank spot. Surprised, Kaigaku laughs at his new ability to talk back at him. Zenitsu asks for why he had become a demon, why someone poised to acquire Thunder Breathing would choose to become a demon, before angrily revealing that Jigoro had committed seppuku because of his defection.
He explains that during seppuku, another person must behead the condemned to prevent prolonged pain. Yet, Jigoro chose to slit his stomach instead of his throat to atone. He died in agony and alone because the wielders of Thunder Breathing had produced a demon. Kaigaku laughs off the news and mockingly asks if he should repent, claiming that he does not care about anyone who doesn't value him. He will always serve those who know his worth and is happy that Jigoro is dead because he wouldn't annoint him his sole successor despite everything he did. "The old bastard said he would make me joint successor with scum like you."
Zenitsu evades Kaigaku's attack.
As he insults their trainer as a senile old man, Zenitsu rejects his words. "If I'm scum, then you're trash! I feel sorry for Grandpa for having such pathetic successors... I can only do the first form and you can do everything except that!" Angered that he would claim they are the same, Kaigaku draws his blade and uses Thunder Breathing, Fourth Form: Distant Thunder. Zenitsu suddenly rushes past him and claims he is too slow. To the Upper Rank's shock, Zenitsu has already slit his neck, with the demon noting that he now moves like a completely different person.
Kaigaku recalls his encounter with Kokushibo.
Kaigaku remembers his encounter with Upper Rank One, believing it was not shameful to kneel before an overwhelmingly strong opponent. To him, as long as he remains alive, it would all work out in the end. It does not matter if dirt is rubbed in his face, he is forced to drink dirty water, or people curse him for stealing money; what mattered was that he was alive and that someday, he would succeed. Kokushibo asks if Kaigaku wants to become a demon and get stronger, drawing blood from his hand to drink. If Muzan recognizes him, he will transform into a demon.
He explains that to become one takes time, a process that is longer the stronger a person is; Kokushibo himself took three days to transform. Additionally, to counteract the effects of Total Concentration, much blood must be drunk, and rarely does a person's body not allow them to become a demon. Kokushibo tells the Demon Slayer to be grateful for the blood he received, threatening to behead him should he spill a drop. He reminisces on the intense fear he felt as he put the blood into his mouth, as if his cells were screaming and crying.
Compared to facing Zenitsu now, the Upper Rank is not worried. Despite gaining some strength, he believes Zenitsu remains a worthless coward, crying without dignity or perseverance. He recalls when Jigoro had offered to make them both his successors and curses his former trainer for comparing him to his junior. As he angrily declares that they both deserved to die, Kaigaku uses Thunder Breathing, Second Form: Rice Spirit, attacking Zenitsu with five consecutive slashes and injuring his face. Zenitsu remarks that with the consecutive attacks, Kaigaku has already eaten much victims, believing he can't tell good from evil anymore.
Kaigaku wounds Zenitsu with Sixth Form: Rumble and Flash.
Kaigaku responds he does know, as he uses Third Form: Thunder Swarm to weave around Zenitsu and injure him further. He explains his belief that those who know his worth are good and those who don't are evil. Using Fifth Form: Heat Lightning, Kaigaku slashes and burns Zenitsu simultaneously, asking if he enjoys his blade infused with his Blood Demon Art, before attacking him again with Sixth Form: Rumble and Flash, wounding Zenitsu all throughout his body; Kaigaku gloats that with his immense power both burning and slashing him, he has become a demon to surpass Thunder Breathing.
As Zenitsu falls, with the demon remarking he is truly different to him, he recalls when Jigoro once pointed to Kaigaku as an example. Thunder Breathing as a style revolves around using the first form as a foundation; as such, it didn't matter if someone that used the other forms when they couldn't do the first. Knowing this, he recalls that even when Kaigaku was a lesser user of the style, he retained an arrogant personality, dismissing anyone who he perceived to be beneath him, despite himself knowing that Kaigaku could never be a Hashira as a result.
He understands why Kaigaku hates him, but despite also returning the sentiment, he still respected Kaigaku for his hard work. To him and Jigoro, Kaigaku was a special person, yet none of it satisfied him. He compares Kaigaku's heart to a box with a hole that held his happiness; despite whatever went in, it could never fill up.
Zenitsu beheads Kaigaku using Seventh Form: Honoikazuchi no Kami.
Apologizing to Jigoro for the two of them taking different paths, he uprights his body and plants his feet along the wall to stop his descent. As Kaigaku watches with surprise, Zenitsu apologizes to him and attacks with Thunder Breathing, Seventh Form: Honoikazuchi no Kami, instantly decapitating Upper Rank Six. As he plummets, Kaigaku tries to comprehend what had just happened, unable to see the attack. He curses Jigoro for favoring Zenitsu by teaching him an exclusive form, but Zenitsu denies their trainer was such a person. This form was of his creation, one he had hoped to use to fight alongside him.
Yushiro taunts Kaigaku for his lonely death, before saving Zenitsu.
After Zenitsu beheads Kaigaku with Thunder Breathing, Seventh Form: Honoikazuchi no Kami, both fall in the Infinity Castle to their deaths. Zenitsu plummets while unconscious as the disintegrating Kaigaku grows furious at his defeat by Zenitsu's hand, angered that the one he believed to be weaker than himself had managed to create a seventh form. He comforts himself with the idea that he too will die with him when he hits the bottom.
Suddenly Yushiro enters Kaigaku's vision, telling him that those who never give anything will one day never gain from others, and that only wanting is the same as having nothing when they cannot create for others, before coldly telling the fallen Upper Rank that it is pitiful to die alone. Yushiro leaps across the walls and catches the unconscious Zenitsu, while the fallen Upper Rank disintegrates to ash, marking a pathetic end to the prideful and traitorous Demon Slayer.
Zenitsu see himself in the afterlife, a land full of red spider lilies; he sees his master Jigoro across the Sanzu River, separating the two. He apologizes to him for never getting along with Kaigaku despite his attempts to reach out, believing if it wasn't for him, Kaigaku wouldn't have been goaded into becoming a demon. He apologizes for never repaying his debts, and adds that he truly wanted to become a Hashira whilst he was alive. However, Jigoro remains silent, and Zenitsu, believing he still hates him, asks for his trainer to say something to him.
Suddenly, the lilies begin to wrap around his feet, pulling him into the ground. Watches as he sinks lower, Jigoro tearfully informs his former student, "Zenitsu... I'm proud of you", causing him to tear up as well. In reality, Zenitsu awakens to Yushiro patching his wounds, surrounded and guarded by more Demon Slayer. Murata, who recognizes him, asks on his condition and whether he can be saved. Annoyed by his yelling and begging, Yushiro only tells him to keep on guard.
Yushiro telling Murata that his screams draws the attention of several demons.
Murata does not taken kindly to his orders and demands to know his rank but the demon ignores him while administering a styptic to stop Zenitsu's bleeding, though he notes that the cuts on his face might worsen. Murata chastises him for his pessimism and comforts Zenitsu, as the others tell him he will be saved as well. Yushiro remarks was lucky that Kaigaku had not mastered his techniques, saying he could have killed him had he progressed in a years. Murata once again demands he keep positive, but his screaming draws the attention of several demons.
Yushiro, the only demon to not be created by Muzan Kibutsuji, recalls when Tamayo had told him to act naturally as he assisted the Demon Slayers, though his dissatisfaction was plainly written on his face. After changing his eye color and donning a uniform, the others did not suspect Yushiro to be a demon, though they sensed that something was not right. Murata struggles to sever a demon's neck, causing Yushiro to demand he hasten his effort. He uses a Kasugai crow with his talisman to sense his surroundings, but grows concerned when something is nearby.
Tanjiro becomes enraged to see Akaza again.
As Tanjiro and Giyu continue through the castle, he notices they have not encountered any Upper Ranks, before wondering on the whereabouts of Muzan and the other Hashira. As he tries to tell himself they will succeed, the hallway they are in begins to shake violently as something approaches them. He wonders if it is a battle but senses it is approaching them, recognizing its scent. Giyu warns him to stay back as the ceiling cracks open; Akaza lands down to face the two and taunts Tanjiro, surprised that someone as weak as him is still alive, before lunging at Tanjiro while yelling his name. Angered to see the familiar face, Tanjiro dodges and yells out his name in return, ready to fight Upper Rank Three.
Elsewhere, hovering above a bottomless shaft, Tamayo finds herself trapped in a fleshy cocoon. Noticing it is able to decompose her human-conversion drug, she realizes it will absorb her as well in enough time and pleads for someone to save her.
Tengen and Shinjuro guard the Ubuyashikis.
While in the process of mapping out the Infinity Castle, Kanata begins to envision the recently deceased members of her family. Her emotions begin to overwhelm her and her eyes well up with tears, but Kiriya tells her to stop crying and continue with her task, reassuring her that they will win. Kanata acknowledges his orders and recomposes herself to continue. Sitting outside the room of the Ubuyashikis are the former Hashiras Tengen Uzui and Shinjuro Rengoku. Tengen marvels at Kiriya's mental fortitude, continuing his mission despite the lingering anguish of his father's death.
Shinjuro agrees and is amazed that children so young have taken on an enormous responsibility. He promises to risk his life to protect them, as Kyojuro did, in order to no longer bring shame to his family name. Elsewhere in the estate, Sakonji tends to an unconscious Nezuko; despite using Tamayo's human-conversion drug on her as told, she seems to be in pain, sweating profusely and groaning. He notes that if she truly can be human again, Muzan's scheme will fall apart, losing the only demon in a thousand years to ever be resistant to sunlight.
However, Sakonji himself is also trembling and sweating in sheer nervousness. Whenever he thinks about the battle's eventual endgame, he grows anxious to realize the ancient war of humans and demons might soon end, something he will witness. He reminisces on Tanjiro and realizes he had always played a pivotal part. Since bringing his sister to him, Sakonji had felt as if cogs had begun to turn. The ancient war is but a giant machine, and with the introduction of him and Nezuko, it is as if two added cogs have shifted the stagnant situation to begin moving. He hopes that the siblings will not lose.
Tanjiro evades Akaza's punch using Hinokami Kagura: Fire Wheel.
As Akaza throws a punch at Tanjiro, the Demon Slayer performs Hinokami Kagura: Fire Wheel to flip over him and catch his arm with his blade. He summons the strength to slice it off, but Akaza regenerates it back and quickly retaliates by swinging his fist back at his head. Using Hinokami Kagura: Fake Rainbow, he evades the blow and appears behind the demon, while also managing to slash through his head. Giyu is impressed to see Tanjiro has progressed in his technique so much, as Akaza stares curiously at his attacker; he remarks that he can confidently say his ability is now that of a Hashira's to be able to handle an Upper Rank.
Giyu becomes amazed by Tanjiro's rapid progression.
On the first day they met, all Tanjiro could do was despair in his weakness and beg for Nezuko's life to be spared; now able to fight, Tanjiro won't ever again lose his life or his dignity. Akaza suddenly remembers Kyojuro's words, "This boy is not weak. Do not insult him", and realizes now he was telling the truth. He remarks that Tanjiro is certainly no longer weak, and to show he has earned his respect, Upper Rank Three performs Technique Development, Destructive Death: Compass Needle, to celebrate his opponent's new strength in a battle.
Giyu blocks Akaza's Disorder with Eleventh Form: Dead Calm.
Using Water Breathing, Third Form: Flowing Dance, Giyu maneuvers around Akaza and evades his numerous attacks; Akaza remarks that it had been fifty years since he fought a Water Hashira, using Destructive Death: Disorder to force him to retaliate. Giyu uses Water Breathing, Eleventh Form: Dead Calm to dispel the shockwaves; Akaza becomes impressed, having never seen the technique as the last Water Hashira he had killed did not use it. Tanjiro attacks him from behind, using Hinokami Kagura: Raging Sun to go for his neck.
Akaza evades the slashes and appears behind him, attempt to chop off his head. He fails to perform Hinokami Kagura: Fake Rainbow in time but is saved when Giyu slashes off the Upper Rank's arm with Water Breathing, Second Form: Water Wheel, though he regenerates the limb instantly. The two clash head on; attacking again from behind him, Tanjiro tries using Hinokami Kagura: Flame Dance to cut down the demon but Akaza uses Destructive Death: Leg Type, Crown Splitter to fend him off. He blocks the attack with his sword but his nose still bleeds from the sheer force of Akaza's kick.
Akaza launches Giyu with Leg Type: Explosive Flurry.
As Akaza evades Giyu's slashes, he marvels at his superb technique and demands to know his name, wishing to remember. Giyu refuses to divulge his name to the demon and tells him he hates talking; the amused Akaza responds that he enjoys talking in battle and decides he will continually ask for it instead. Using Destructive Death: Leg Type, Explosive Flurry, Akaza kicks at Giyu in rapid succession and launches him away with his shockwaves; despite blocking the attack with his sword's handle, Giyu is sent flying through numerous walls.
Burning Bones, Summer Sun clashes with Eight-Layered Demon Core.
Tanjiro attempts to call out to Giyu but Akaza appears before him, satisfied to know the Hashira's name. The Demon Slayer and Upper Three clash, with Tanjiro performing Hinokami Kagura: Burning Bones, Summer Sun and Akaza retaliating with Destructive Death: Eight-Layered Demon Core. The attack's vibrations ring loudly in his sword but Tanjiro is able to escape the attack unharmed. Akaza compliments him for his growth and his training to reach his level. He commends Kyojuro for Tanjiro's success, recalling their first encounter when he was lying on the ground too weak to be notices, but as of right now, he is happy and excited to battle him.
He tells Tanjiro he is glad that Kyojuro is dead, believing he had already reached his peak because he valued being human. Upon hearing the demon's statement, Tanjiro becomes furious and demands he take back his words. Confused, Akaza responds he is praising the two of them, but Tanjiro retorts he is only insulting those he calls weak. The demon believes Tanjiro misunderstands him and states that he only despises the weak because it disgusts him; to him, it is the law of nature to weed out the weak.
Tanjiro tells Akaza that him standing now is proof he is wrong; everyone begins life as a baby, born weak and needing help from someone, including him. He states that the true law of nature is that the strong protect the weak, and the weak become stronger to help those less than them; telling Akaza his way of thinking is unforgivable, he declares his days of doing what he pleases are over, causing the demon to clench his fist in anger.
Facing off against Tanjiro, Akaza cannot brush aside the repulsive feeling he is giving him. He is unsure why he feels angry fighting him since he knows Tanjiro is no longer weak, yet he cannot shake the feeling of his eyes, voice and words cutting into him. At that moment, someone seemingly grabs Akaza's shoulder and confirms Tanjiro's words; everyone starts off weak, then they get help from everyone around them and learn, but that he should only compare his own progress against himself, not that of others.
The man tells him what is important is becoming stronger than he was yesterday, and by developing himself, soon he can be the one to help people. Angered, Akaza tries to punch behind him to hit the man, but strikes nothing. As a bewildered Tanjiro sees Akaza punch the air suddenly, Upper Rank Three angrily mutters, "Tanjiro, you really are unpleasant".
Akaza attacks Tanjiro with Flying Planet Thousand Wheels.
Akaza suddenly lunges at Tanjiro and uses Destructive Death: Crushing Type, Ten-Thousand Leaves Flashing Willow, rupturing the ground around him, with Tanjiro just barely dodging the attack. As he becomes stunned to see Akaza's new speed and precision, the demon quickly engages the Demon Slayer again from below and uses his Destructive Death: Leg Type, Flying Planet Thousand Wheels, with Tanjiro enduring the blow and vomiting blood as a result. Akaza swings at him but Tanjiro barely ducks down to avoid it, all while he tries to rationalize how the Upper Rank's attacks are so potent.
With his techniques possessing unparalleled precision, as if his fists are magnetized to his vital areas, he tries to understand what he is gauging his attacks on, thinking back to his battle with Kyojuro to find the answer. Using Hinokami Kagura: Solar Heat Haze, Tanjiro slashes at Akaza's neck; his blade seemingly distorts as it slashes him, despite Akaza believed he dodged it by moving away from it. He is amused to see the unusual technique and asks how he performed it, continuing to attack Tanjiro as the Demon Slayer struggles to fend off the relentless onslaught.
At the Rengoku estate, Senjuro prays to his older brother; a large battle has begun and their father is away to protect the Oyakata, asking that Kyojuro protect him and Tanjiro. He thinks back to the letter he sent to Tanjiro; though it was a trivial matter, he had written to him about a conversation the Sengoku era's Flame Hashira had with a user of Sun Breathing. The swordsman had explained his experience of fighting Muzan, but upon hearing his story, the Hashira lost his confidence. Despite this, Senjuro prays that Tanjiro won't lose, wondering if Kyojuro agrees.
Giyu slashes Akaza's hands to save Tanjiro.
In the midst of the battle, it is revealed that Senjuro's Kasugai Crow has indeed entered the Infinity Castle, but has not given Tanjiro his letter and is watching the battle behind cover, forcing him to defeat Akaza in order to read it. Tanjiro uses Hinokami Kagura: Dance and swings down at the demon, but Akaza catches the blade mid-slash and attempts to break it. In a desperate move, he headbutts Upper Three, but Akaza only compliments him for his efforts.
He kicks Akaza in the chin but he continues to maintain his hold. As the blade begins to creak, Akaza's hands are suddenly slashed off, saving Tanjiro. He looks up and sees Giyu has returned, as the Water Hashira becomes angry at the severe pain in his back from being launched by Akaza.
As Giyu and Akaza face each other, Giyu rationalizes why he fights as an individual. Though he is usually hesitant to draw his sword and isn't one to fight for amusement, standing now and facing an opponent who can overwhelm him, he realizes his senses have sharpened in a short amount of time; senses that once lie dormant in him and just now are brought out onto the battlefield he stands on. He finally understands the intense struggle to increase one's own skills; as Tanjiro looks on, the Water Hashira manifests a splash-like mark on his cheek.
A Marked Giyu attacks Akaza with Fourth Form: Striking Tide.
Giyu makes a powerful swing at Akaza, just barely missing his mark. The demon responds with a punch straight to his head but Giyu ducks down and slashes his neck, forcing Akaza to back away. Tanjiro notes that with his Mark manifested, Giyu's speed has increased greatly; the Hashira uses Water Breathing, Fourth Form: Striking Tide and attacks Upper Three head-on, splitting the demon's arm but sustaining a gash to his head. Watching from a distance, Tanjiro notes that despite both fighters moving at tremendous speeds, Akaza was able to quickly adapt to Giyu's enhanced abilities.
Realizing that a lengthy battle will decided by a demon's endless strength and that their true goal is defeating Muzan, he scrambles to find a way to beat Akaza. He tries to understand how the demon attacks so precisely and is able to react to attacks he cannot immediately see. Recalling when Akaza had complimented Kyojuro on his highly developed fighting spirit, he attempts to define what it is and recalls a conversation he had with Inosuke.
In the Butterfly Mansion, Inosuke informs Tanjiro he feels a tingle where an opponent is aiming at him, which Tanjiro surmises is the reason he was able to survive when Gyutaro had stabbed him from behind. He claims that even when someone is behind him, he can determine where they are looking; as a demonstration, he asks Tanjiro to look at his back, upon which he correctly answers that he was looking at his right shoulder. Inosuke adds that when someone looks at him with the intent to kill, he can tell immediately.
Remembering this moment, Tanjiro realizes Inosuke was able to do so because of his honed sense of touch. At the same time, Inosuke had angrily remarked that if someone isn't looking at him with hostility, he cannot sense them; he points out the old woman at the Wisteria House, as she once sat behind Inosuke without him able to detect her. He believes that if he was able to get close to an opponent without emitting hostility, they wouldn't be able to detect him. However, Tanjiro added that while an elderly lady had no reason to harm him, it would be impossible to kill a demon without showing hostility.
Akaza catches Tanjiro's sword without looking.
Despite remembering the moment as a silly conversation, he realizes it was still able to help him learn. What Akaza senses is something he calls "fighting spirit" but he remains unsure of what it is exactly and whether he can use it to disrupt Akaza's Compass Needle. As the two continue to clash, Akaza parries Giyu's blade, throwing him off-balance and attempting to throw a punch. Tanjiro goes for his exposed neck and uses Hinokami Kagura: Dance, but the Upper Rank grabs his sword from behind him and throws a punch with his other hand, mocking Tanjiro for leaving himself open.
He is barely able to dodge the blow and sustains a cut across his stomach. Giyu engages him again as Tanjiro backs away, attempting to find what Akaza is sensing until he has an epiphany.
Tanjiro remembers how his father seemed like a plant; he was never temperamental and was always calm, maintaining his demeanor until his death. Whenever he remembers him, he immediately thinks of his gentle smile and calming voice. Tanjiro recalls a time he had asked him about what he thinks when he performs the Hinokami Kagura. Even as a child, Tanjiro knew that the practice was physically demanding, as it involved performing all twelve forms from sunset to sunrise continuously. Worried about his frail body, Tanjiro asks if he can be the one to do it next year.
Tanjuro thanks his son for his concern but brushes aside his worry, stating that in the last few years he performed it, he never believed it to be difficult. He remembers learning it from his own father, but comments that even though he was younger and healthier back then, doing it exhausted him greatly. He surmised it was because the forms had unnecessary movements; instead, what matters was maintaining proper breathing and control, making the most efficient moves to exert the most strength. Tanjuro states that by doing this, your mind gradually becomes clear.
In the beginning, he must learn to pick up the movements and sensibilities to open all his senses and become conscious of his own body, down to his very blood vessels. It is this process that is extremely strenous and presents the most self-doubt in himself, maybe even believing that he will not succeed despite his progress. After gaining the knowledge, he will know to remove what is unnecessary and close himself off. Eventually, he can control the vessels and muscles in his body as easily as blinking, and once he clears his head, he will see the Transparent World, though only through pushing himself to his strength limits. When Tanjiro asks if he can attain it, Tanjuro reassures him that he can with diligent work, before presenting him with new warajis.
Tanjuro confronts a bear threatening his family.
Ten days before Tanjuro's death, a bear had come to the mountain they lived in and killed people. As the Kamado family sleeps through a blizzard, Tanjuro suddenly awakens and gets up from, after which he asks his eldest son to accompany him. As Tanjuro and a still sleepy Tanjiro wandered outside, the two encounter the bear, standing almost nine shaku tall and believed to have killed six people. Hiding behind a tree,  Tanjiro watches his father confront the bear despite his illness and armed with only an axe; they had strung ropes with bells attached as a warning but his father knew it was nearby without hearing them.
Tanjuro apologizes for its hunger but warns the creature not to come any closer; if anything tries to harm his family, he will show it no mercy and take its life. As the bear roars and lumbers forward to kill him, Tanjuro swings his axe and leaps up, decapitating the bear before it could move a step. As its giant head drops to the ground, Tanjiro tries to piece together what had happened; in that moment, Tanjuro would have had to swing twice to get completely through its neck, and with his sense of smell, he realizes he never wavered in the slightest.
Tanjiro enters the Transparent World.
Before and after killing it, he showed no fear, no ill will, and maintained his usual calm self. As he turns to ask if his son had observed him, Tanjiro answers that he did and hugs him; Tanjuro tells him to remember the events of today. Looking back at that night, he realizes his father had given him a lesson to see the Transparent World, much like his descendants before him had to learn. It is then he understands his father's advice and how he was able to dodge Akaza's potentially lethal strike.
For just an instant, when the demon grabbed his blade and was poised to swing, Tanjiro had entered the Transparent World, his vision was heightened and he could see Akaza's muscles through his body. Managing to close off his other senses to dodge something unavoidable, his body became even faster. Realizing he should have never doubted Inosuke for his advice, he resolves to take down Akaza whilst he battles Giyu.
Tanjiro sees Akaza with the Transparent World.
Having seen the Transparent World momentarily, Tanjiro realizes his own perception and speed have increased dramatically; he was able to predict Akaza's attacks and evade them. His breathing and the flow of his blood became visible to him, and he even saw his own muscles contract; he determines that by closing off his Fighting Spirit, he may be able to behead him.
As the now desperate Giyu uses Water Breathing, Tenth Form: Constant Flux against Akaza, the demon only sustains a shallow cut to his neck, while the Hashira is wounded in his shoulder. He notes that making any powerful attack on Akaza will only responded to with equal force, leaving him nowhere to go when his attempts to attack him are now predictable. He marvels at the sheer power of Upper Rank Three, a killing machine whose only purpose is to fight.
Akaza snaps Giyu's blade.
As Akaza taunts Giyu for using all of his forms, he prepares to end the battle and expresses surprise he has lasted thus far. Tanjiro, watching as Akaza gets close to Giyu, observes the demon and attempts to concentrate. Giyu slashes down on the demon's neck, but Akaza intercepts the slash, using his fist to break off the Hashira's Nichirin katana. Shocked at his weapon breaking, Giyu stands helplessly as Akaza bids him goodbye and aims a punch at his chest. Blood sprays from his hand is but it is Akaza's own, his hand has been suddenly sliced off as Tanjiro uses Hinokami Kagura to save Giyu, who notes that the sound of his breathing has changed.
Akaza uses Final Form: Blue Silver Chaotic Afterglow.
Observing the Demon Slayer as he stands to face him, Akaza grows alarmed as he senses the changed Tanjiro is now exceedingly dangerous. Using Technique Development, Final Form: Blue Silver Chaotic Afterglow, Upper Three summons his Compass Needle and launches numerous explosives shockwaves in an omni-direction attack. Giyu panics at his increased power and speed; he wonders if he can negate it with Dead Calm, but now seeing into the Transparent World, Tanjiro instead wonders if time has slowed or Giyu and Akaza have.
Though he uses his eleventh form, Giyu sustains severe wounds across his body as the shockwaves pass through his defensive stance. Akaza is impressed to see the Water Hashira survive the attack and offers to transform him into a demon, telling not to die like Kyojuro and Tanjiro. Instead, Giyu is stunned to see Tanjiro standing behind the Upper Rank, who is now unable to sense him. As Tanjiro looks at Akaza's neck, he angrily calls out the demon's name, causing Giyu to chide him for giving away his position. Akaza swings but Tanjiro evades the punch and goes for an attack.
Tanjiro beheads Akaza with Setting Sun Transformation.
Initially surprised Tanjiro has survived his attack, he pays no attention and believes his Compass Needle will sense him. However, he is unable to sense anything as his Fighting Spirit is now absent. Taken aback at first, Akaza composes himself and waits for the attack to be detected, but Tanjiro has already used Hinokami Kagura: Setting Sun Transformation and beheaded the Upper Rank, much to his and Giyu's shock.
Akaza compares fighting Tanjiro to fighting a plant.
After being beheaded by Tanjiro, Akaza reflects on the moment; in the last few hundred years, he had never seen someone without Fighting Spirit; even a baby crying shows it is fighting to live. Tanjiro's Fighting Spirit had disappeared completely, like he was fighting a plant, an anomaly that should not exist and caused his Compass to not respond. Still, he pushes past the challenge of not sensing Tanjiro, knowing that in battle, it is vital to immediately understand and handle the unexpected.
Yet, he understood that Tanjiro had grasped something and surpassed his speed, attacking head-on to defeat hundreds of years of martial arts experience. His eyes bored no malice or Fighting Spirit and Akaza realizes he had perceived the "Domain of Supremacy", a Selfless State whose vague existence was something he knew but could never have attained.
Akaza puts his detached head back onto his body and attempts to heal, vowing to keep fighting and get stronger. Tanjiro realizes what he is trying to do and Giyu responds by hurling his broken sword at the demon's head, knocking it away from his body. Despite his head now separated, Akaza still attempts to will himself and continue getting stronger, but the head begins to disintegrate to ash, eventually leaving Giyu's sword where it lands. Tanjiro grows relieved as he sees he has won, but his body begin to tremble from reaching his limit.
Akaza uses Compass Needle despite his decapitation.
However, the two notice Akaza's body has not faded yet. As they look on in anxious anticipation, his body suddenly performs Technique Development: Compass Needle and takes a fighting stance, the neck staunching its wound to stop the bleeding.  The headless body attacks Tanjiro and attempt to chop off his neck, only barely missing when he dodges the blow. As it attempts to grow a new head, it kicks Tanjiro in the side and sends him crashing into a wall. In pain and shock, Tanjiro questions how he could've failed to kill Akaza despite beheading him.
Despite his wounds, Giyu vows to protect Tanjiro from Akaza.
He initially believes he has a special condition, as with Gyutaro and Daki, but remembering how he saw the severed head burn to ash; instead, Akaza is attempting to evolve even further, and like Muzan, he is trying to extend his weakness beyond his head. As he attempts to getting up, Tanjiro finally loses consciousness after having reached his body's limit. Watching from behind them and see him vulnerable, Giyu picks up his broken sword and uses Water Breathing, Fourth Form: Striking Tide, but the headless body heals the slashes almost instantly.
Without his Mark, Giyu is quickly overwhelmed by Akaza's attacks and is brought down. The demon turns to Tanjiro with the intent to kill but the Hashira yells at the demon that he is still alive, and if he wants to get to Tanjiro, he must defeat him first. A voice rings in Akaza, telling him that indomitable wills won't ever break in any hardship, and that while "they" are not samurai who carry a sword, they carry swords in their heart and use their fists. Akaza disregards the voice as a nuisance and attempts to confront Giyu, but he is held back by a young woman, who tearfully tells him, "Hakuji, that's enough."
As Giyu readies to fight Akaza once more, he realizes the direness of his situation; his left ear hearing is gone, his right hand is numb, and he can't tell how much strength he has left. As with how sprinting can only be done for so long till the point of exhaustion, reaching past one's physical limits results in precision being lost and heavy strain on the muscles, hands, and feet. Demons on the other hand, don't feel pain, nor do they tired; it is a miracle anyone can battle an Upper Rank with just a Breathing Style. Despite the odds, Giyu resolves to save Tanjiro and prevent the death of another person who saved him.
Akaza is stopped by the hallucination of a woman.
The woman urges Akaza to stop and holds onto his hand, who demands she let go and asks who she is. She begs him to leave but the demon wishes to kill Giyu and Tanjiro. When asked why he wants to kill them, he answers that he must become stronger, and when the woman asks why he must, Akaza responds, "Because... if I'm not strong, I can't bring it back. Medicine for my father." As his life flashes before his eyes, he remembers he wanted to get stronger so that he could steal money, fight back against his victims when they retaliate, and endure beatings at the magistrate's office when he is caught.
A young Hakuji is beaten for stealing.
Tied up and bloody from his lashings, Akaza, then known as Hakuji, is presented before the magistrate, who warns him after getting tattooed for his crimes, the next punishment is losing a hand. Hakuji laughs and dismisses the threat, claiming that without hands, he can still use his feet, vowing to never get caught again. The magistrate reminds him even at the age of eleven, he is already a repeat offender and endures beatings severe enough to make a grown man faint, calling him a 'demon child'. After leaving the office, Hakuji laughs off being insulted as a demon child and claims he was born with teeth. Suddenly, a man informs him that his father had hung himself upon learning he was caught.
At the cemetery, holding a letter from him in his hand, he finds his father's headstone. The letter he wrote to him reads: "Dear Hakuji. Live a righteous life. You can still change. I didn't want to live if it meant stealing from people. I am sorry for troubling you". Clutching his headstone, Hakuji mourns his father, angrily asking if the poor were even allowed to live and cursing the world for his death.
A grieving Hakuji releases his rage at a group of strangers.
Hurt and enraged, Hakuji walked into a town and started a brawl, brutally beating several men as they tried to fight back against him, all while denouncing them for being alive as his father dies. He yells out that he wasn't a bother who needed to apologize for anything, and for his sake, he could take any punishment they give him no matter the severity. His father's condition had begun to worsen but he was sure he could save him, yet he chose to hang himself and die, a choice he was prepared to make himself and do for him. As his victims lay unconscious and Hakuji takes time to breathe, a martial artist offers him a slow clap and commends his skill. He notes he had been summoned with the news that a child was about to be killed, only to instead see that said child has knocked seven grown men unconscious.
The man tells Hakuji he has promise and is impressed by his skill to fight bare-handed; Akaza wonders who he is as he realizes he is seeing his memories. When the man asks if he could come to his dojo since he has no students, Hakuji angrily dismisses his offer and threatens to kill him. He notes that he has tattoos branding him as a criminal from Edo, meaning he was banished and came here, but Hakuji pays no heed and claims it has nothing to do with him. The man tells him it is time he is reborn and takes a fighting stance; Hakuji lunges at him with all his rage but the man throws numerous rapid punches at the boy, knocking him unconscious.
When he regains consciousness, the man is amazed at his toughness despite the severe beating he received, only waking up after an hour. He introduces himself as Keizo, a martial teacher at a dojo that teaches the Soryu Style, though he earns a living through odd jobs due to having no students. As Hakuji follows behind him, Keizo explains his new job is to nurse his sick daughter whilst he is away; his wife grew tired of having to care for her and drowned herself, and burdened by her death, he became weak-willed. Hakuji questions if Keizo would want a criminal to care for his daughter, but Keizo notes that since he had defeated him, it is okay with him now.
Akaza meets Koyuki.
It is then that Akaza realizes the reason he dislikes Tanjiro is because he reminds him of Keizo, a figment of his worthless life's story. Keizo introduces him to his daughter Koyuki, and her condition reminds Hakuji of his father's own illness. He asks if she is feeling better than before and introduces her to the boy behind him, who refuses to give his name. Keizo asks that she get it before he comes back and leaves to go to work. Alone with Hakuji, Koyuki asks if he is okay, seeing his injuries; Akaza remarks that his worthless life was nothing but lies.
Koyuki apologizes for burdening Hakuji, which he does not mind.
Hakuji questions why the ill are always apologizing for what they can't control. They want independence, but cannot move, and despite suffering, they blame themselves. While helping Koyuki, she apologizes because he is unable to train or have fun with her; her condition had worsened, leading to him spending all night changing her bedding and towels, giving her water, and helping her relieve herself. However, having helped his father with his illness and with superior endurance to most, Hakuji was not bothered.
He tells Koyuki he spends his time training anyway and does not mind staying in. She insists that he leave her sometimes, having heard there would be fireworks tonight and insisting he go. He responds he can simply carry her and they can go see them together. She becomes confused, and he explains that even if she can't go today, they will be on each year and she can go see them then. Upon hearing this, Koyuki begins to cry; dismayed, Hakuji notes it is the one thing he didn't like about nursing her, believing that being sick and bedridden was making her sad, something he didn't enjoy.
While taking a drink with Keizo, the master notes that the kanji for "Haku" in Hakuji is the same as "Koma" in Komainu, believing that both of them must protect something like a Komainu protecting its shrine, a fact that makes him laugh. Hakuji recounts how Keizo came to own the dojo; though he wasn't a samurai, he owned the land because he had saved the owner from bandits. Impressed with his fighting and without an heir, the man gave Keizo his land and dojo. However, others who wanted the land were displeased Keizo took ownership; a nearby kenjutsu dojo began to harass Keizo's dojo, leading him to have difficulty finding students. Despite this, lessons with him and helping Koyuki healed Keizo's heart.
Keizo asks Hakuji if he would be his successor to the dojo.
Years later, Hakuji is now eighteen and Koyuki is sixteen. No longer sick, she was bright, cheery, and eager to help in the dojo, happy to live normally. One day, Keizo calls Hakuji over to the main room, where he asks if Hakuji would like to be his successor to the dojo, adding that Koyuki likes him, rendering both teens speechless. Having been branded a criminal, he never imagined himself with a future, let alone one where someone likes him. He realizes he is now able to live the righteous life his father had asked, giving him the hope that he could start anew. Hakuji bowed in gratitude to Keizo, recalling at that moment, he would give his life to Koyuki and Keizo, and as such, he could have never imagined them poisoned to death.
Hakuji went to his father's grave to tell him he would be getting married, but while returning, he saw people at the front of the dojo, giving him a terrible premonition. He is told that the well they drank from was poisoned, because the assailant couldn't beat him or Keizo in a battle. Inside the dojo, Hakuji saw the bodies of Koyuki and Keizo, their clothes bloody and faces covered. He lamented that once more, a crisis has happened and he wasn't there to save the people he loved, even when he promised. Previously, while watching a display of fireworks, Koyuki asked him if he had remembered when they both talked about seeing them, to which he vaguely recalls.
She tells him that even such a minor conversation made her happy, because even when she couldn't see them then, he had told her she could see them next year. Koyuki couldn't imagine living another year; her mother felt the same way, which she believes is the reason she killed herself. She knew that even her father had given up on her because she was so weak. Despite it, she remarks when he told her about the coming years, it was as if Hakuji could see her future and stated it as a matter of fact. She asks if he would be her husband, holding his hand. Hakuji holds hers and says yes, promising to become stronger than anyone else and protect her for life; Hakuji bitterly remarks that in the end, he never lived up to his promise.
Hakuji massacres the rival dojo in a fit of rage and grief.
Records at the magistrate's office recount details of a gruesome massacre; enraged at losing the people he loved once again, Hakuji attacked the kenjutsu dojo and killed 67 of its members with his bare hands. The dojo was strewn with crushed organs and bodies mangled beyond recognition, a hellish scene with viscera, brains, and limbs scattered along the walls and ceiling. The maid who witnessed the massacre lost her mind, and thirty years later, the records were destroyed because it was so unbelievable, it was thought to be fabricated.
Muzan impales Hakuji's head.
Bloodied and dazed, Hakuji walked mindlessly until he came to a footbridge. The man on it remarks about hearing of the dojo's massacre and was curious as he didn't recall sending a demon to the town, disappointed to know it was a human who committed the murders. Hakuji threatens to kill the stranger when he suddenly lunges and impales his head with his hand. Planning to create a group of twelve powerful demons, he asks Hakuji if he could withstand the blood he will received. Broken by his loss, he replies that he did not care anymore.
As a demon, now going by the name Akaza, Hakuji has lost his memories but was still drawn to seeking greater strength, even when he had nothing he wanted to protect. He didn't want to live in a world without his family, and for over the next century, he would go on to commit countless acts of senseless violence, denouncing his entire life as "a horribly sad, laughable, and ridiculous story."
As Akaza laments being unable to go to heaven like his father, Keizo and Koyuki, he becomes furious that Tanjiro and Giyu have reminded him of his painful past. He curses humans as weak, soft, and brittle; they die easily, they're brittle, and disappear into nothing. Tanjiro awakens from his ordeal, shocked at how he fainted. Akaza begins to regenerate his head and performs Destructive Death: Annihilation Type. As Tanjiro yells at him to stop, the demon is shocked that he has managed to survive his kick. Declaring that he will behead the demon again, Tanjiro's sword ignites with the fires of the Hinokami Kagura.
However, his sword slips out of his grasp, forcing Tanjiro to punch Akaza's face instead, reminding him of when he first met Keizo. Akaza recalls why he hates weak people; they don't fight face to face, they poison wells, and they're impatient, and he killed these weak people with his fists. He then realizes that throughout his demon life, he turned Keizo's fighting style into a weapon and disrespected his father's last words, finally realizing who he must truly kill. As Tanjiro panics about his lost sword and sees Akaza about to use the same technique that killed Kyojuro, he notices Giyu in the attack's range. Despite Giyu telling him to not worry about him, Tanjiro grabs him and throws both themselves out of the technique's path.
Akaza destroys his own body with Annihilation Type.
He then sees Akaza with a slight smile on his face, engulfed by numerous shockwaves. The attack leaves the surrounding area devastated and Akaza's body a broken, bloody mess. Wondering why he would attack himself, Tanjiro smells a scent of gratitude from the corpse, before asking why he had smiled before hitting himself. The body begins to regenerate, but Akaza stops the process, accepting that the fight is over and he had lost. He commends Tanjiro for his magnificent technique, anticipating and slashing before he could react. The broken body begins to walk away, while Akaza's spirit decides he would go to Hell with his dignity. When he stops, to Tanjiro's confusion, his spirit meets with his father's.
Asking if he was alright, his father reassures, calling him Hakuji and thanking him. As he apologizes for being unable to fix himself, his head is held by Keizo, who tells him that they would never abandon him no matter what, despite Akaza not being able to go to heaven with them. As he calls out for his master, Muzan appears, grabbing his head and reminding him to get stronger, to continue fighting. With that, his body regenerates even quicker, and Akaza voices his will to keep his promise and get stronger, declaring once again he will kill everyone. Suddenly, Koyuki touches his face, thanking Hakuji and saying that he has done enough. Though Muzan appears again, calling him Akaza once more, he overcomes Muzan's control and grabs Koyuki's spirit on the verge of tears, once again the human Hakuji.
The death of Upper Rank Three.
He tearfully apologizes for being unable to protect her, for not being there when she needed him, and for not being able to keep his promise. Seeing him crying for forgiveness, Koyuki is glad that Hakuji had remembered them all despite his long demon life and returned as a human again. With the words, "Welcome back, my husband", Akaza stops his regeneration. Tanjiro watches as the body of Upper Three finally fades into ash.
As Hakuji calls out to his father, Keizo and Koyuki that he is back home, his spirit becomes engulfed in the fires of hell, joined by Koyuki. Tanjiro watches as Akaza's body finally fades into nothing, declaring the battle over. Realizing he must reach Tamayo to help her, his body can no longer handle the fatigue and he falls on his face unconscious. Surprised that Tanjiro had suddenly fainted, Giyu tries to call out to him but faints from exhaustion as well, resting his body on his sword. A Kasugai Crow calls out the aftermath of the battle, Tanjiro and Giyu have manage to defeat Upper Three but are now unconscious.
Kokushibo no longer feels Akaza's presence and realizes he has been defeated.
Kokushibo no longer feels Akaza's presence and realizes he has been defeated. Upper One reminisces on his previous vow to kill him, remembering the threat at his life earlier. As he voices that Akaza had opened the path to reach further heights and abandoned it, he grabs his sword and furiously slashes the pillars of his room, cursing him as "exceedingly weak".
Kanao introduces herself to Doma.
Doma sesnses Akaza's demise and comments he felt like a different being that usual. As he brushes aside his comment, he asks for Kanao's name. She introduces herself as Kanao Tsuyuri, adding that she is the little sister of Kanae and Shinobu Kocho. Doma is confused, judging that she doesn't appear blood-related to the two but nonetheless comments that young girls are delicious anyway. While on the subject of eating women, Doma mentions his subordinate's conscious decision to not eat them, owing that fact to his demise.
Despite mentioning that women have more nutritional content to demons that men, Akaza refused and was even given special permission by Muzan to do so, since Akaza was only deployed by Muzan on special missions. As he mourns for the death of his "best friend", Kanao tells him to stop the lies. She figures out Doma does not feel the least bit saddened as the colour on his face stayed the same. When Doma responds back it is due to him being a demon, Kanao retorts by mentioning that demons and humans both circulate blood and the colour of their faces can change.
Kanao states that Kanae felt sorry for Doma due to his apathy.
She mentions that Kanae had felt sorry for him as he feels nothing. She talks about how all people are born with the ability to feel happiness, as well as sadness and anger. Doma cannot understand these feelings, but knowing he was intelligent, Kanao instead tears into how he covers up his lack of feelings with a facade of lies, pretending to experience emotion to hide the fact his heart feels nothing. He feels no happiness, no bitterness, no pain, calling him an empty shell and saying his facade is so comical, it's stupid. Finally she mockingly asks, "Why were you even born?".
Doma's facade drops after Kanao insults him.
Doma comments that throughout his life, he has talked with numerous young women but never a "bully" like Kanao and asks how could she say something so cruel. Kanao retaliates by saying her outright hatred of him, her desire to cut off his head. She changes her opinion of him, "You're not very smart, are you", calling him a disgrace, and smiling as she mentions it was better to kill him as his life is utterly pointless and meaningless.
Doma instantly appears behind her, trying to slice her neck. Kanao reacts in time however and crouches down to slash through his abdomen. When he tries to send out his ice lotuses to hit her, she dodges the incoming attack to safety. As Doma heals, he comments that her reaction speed had accelerated, she is adjusting to his own movement. She has not inhaled any of his ice even though it is extremely difficult to attack in her manner without a breathing technique. Doma suddenly realizes that Kanao might actually be more powerful than Shinobu.
Kanao's anger at Doma.
Kanao feels the goosebumps throughout her body aren't stopping. She evens know to put strength into her fingertips to hold her sword, or risk it shaking. She mentions the demons she had faced in the past pale in comparison to Doma, but she is able to face him due to the immense anger she feels, anger so powerful it feels like her body is burning. She feels she must rampage at him or her body would rip itself apart, the dizziness in her head and her anger turning into hatred. She calls that she hates Doma and asks how he could kill her family.
Doma clashed techniques with Kanao.
Kanao vanishes and instantly appears before him, using the Flower Breathing, Fifth Form: Peonies of Futility to rapidly slash him. Doma comments the consecutive attacks are pretty and retaliates with his Blood Demon Art: Barren Hanging Garden. Kanao attacks back with the Flower Breathing, Second Form: Honorable Shadow Plum to destroy the created ice. Doma notices the key to withstanding his attacks are her eyes. She notices his movements and predicts his next actions in anticipation. Complimenting her as smart and the above-average swordsman, the demon decides the best course of action is to gouge them out. Doma slashes at her face but Kanao bends back, sustaining a small cut on the side of her temple. Using the Flower Breathing, Sixth Form: Whirling Peach, she attacks back at the Upper Rank, who compliments her body and flexibility as well-trained and akin to a spring.
Doma deploys his fearsome Freezing Clouds, forcing Kanao to close her eyes or risk freezing them. While on the defensive, she is attacked again by Doma using Blood Demon Art: Lotus Vines, the ice vines converging on her and forcing Kanao to slice the incoming attack to defend against them. When she is finished cutting them apart, Doma quickly attacks again with his Blood Demon Art: Cold White Princesses, two ice figures of women that spray the icy fog in her direction. Kanao again backs away to avoid the fog but must dodge again when Doma unleashes his Blood Demon Art: Wintry Icicles form from above and nearly impale her.
Doma taunts her for getting away from him, mentioning she needs to get up close to kill him.
Doma taunts her for getting away from him, mentioning that in order to kill him, she needs to get up close. He disappears for a moment and reappears, clutching her Nichirin Sword, despite Kanao aware and anticipating his next moves. Doma mocks her for not holding onto the sword and sticks it near him. He tells the demon slayer to "come and get it", and deploys his Blood Demon Art: Scattering Lotuses in her direction. Kanao forces herself to look through the incoming hail of ice to find the area of minimum damage but sustains multiple cuts to her face.
Suddenly, Inosuke smashes through the roof, announcing, "Out of the sky, Lord-Inosuke's comin' in!", and using Beast Breathing, Fifth Fang: Crazy Cutting, he destroys the incoming wave of ice shards, saving Kanao. He thanks the Kasugai Crow for leading him to the right room.
Inosuke comes to a realization and asks an upset Kanao if Shinobu is dead.
Inosuke looks at Doma's eyes and enthusiastically realizes he is Upper Rank Two. He declares he will defeat him and finally become a Hashira. A confused Doma mentions he isn't hiding his identity as Upper Rank Two. Inosuke sees the injured Kanao and warns her that Shinobu will get angry at seeing her condition. But when Kanao doesn't respond and she becomes upset, Inosuke is stunned into silence. Doma overhears him and mentions that Shinobu will live forever inside him, as "That's how everyone I eat gets saved".
Inosuke is shocked, remembering a memory he had where Shinobu pinky-promised him to not remove the bandage of his injured hand. Inosuke angrily declares, "I'll gnaw you to shreds, trash", and charges towards Doma, despite Kanao warning him not to inhale the cold air he creates. Using his Beast Breathing, Fourth Fang: Slice 'n' Dice, Inosuke slashes at Doma, the demon commenting on his "messed up technique" as well as noticing his chipped blades and unorthodox fighting style. When Doma attempts to slash at Inosuke's neck, he flips back and deflects the fan with his feet, earning a compliment from the Upper Rank for his flexibility and intrigued by his mask. Inosuke lands next to Kanao and presents her with her blade, stolen from an unaware Doma, to her shock. Doma comments that the Demon Slayer is fast and grows more ice to attack, only for Inosuke to deflect them back and kick him in the stomach, knocking him away.
Inosuke manages to slash Doma across both eyes.
As he compliments him again, Inosuke charges forward and readies a slash. Doma comments that the attack is far from the sword's range, so when the boar-headed fighter swings, he become shocked that the attack had reached him and slashes across his eyes. Inosuke had used Beast Breathing, Ninth Fang: Extending Bendy Slash, dislocating the joints of his arm to extend his range. He relocates the bones of his arm but is angered that the new attack's inaccuracy made him missed Doma's head, to Kanao's shock.
Doma is amused at his unusual opponent and comments that throughout his own long life, he had never met a fighter like him. Inosuke takes the compliment and says it's because "the other riff-raff losers are nothing compared to me". But while Inosuke is talking, his mask instantly disappears from his face, surprising him and shocking Kanao. Doma had stolen it without either Demon Slayer noticing and comments the boar skin is quite old. As Inosuke angrily demands his mask back, Doma suddenly responds that he knows and has seen Inosuke's face before.
Doma asks if he and Inosuke had met in the past
Doma asks if he and Inosuke had met in the past, causing Inosuke angrily retorts his statement and demand his hands off his mask. However, Doma is sure they have and that he knows him from somewhere. Inosuke responds again that he has not met Doma before. Doma mentions the one he encountered before was Shinobu, leading Inosuke to comment that he felt as if he had met her before, hoping to ask her the next time they met. When Kanao attempts to lead Inosuke away, saying Doma is spouting random nonsense, Doma becomes surprised and offended, stating his only saving grace is his seriousness and long and clear memory, even during his human years. With that, Doma pierces his own skull with his finger, to Kanao and Inosuke's shock and disgust. He fiddles with his brain until he reaches a particular memory and retells it to the two.
Doma remember the first time he meets Kotoha.
Fifteen years ago, there was a young woman with a baby, roughly 17-18 years of age. She was abused by her husband and mother-in-law daily and encountered Doma's Eternal Paradise Faith. She had no siblings or parents and had no place else to go to. When Doma first met her, her face was severely swollen from the beatings, commenting it was "pretty rough" even to him, and that the woman was even partially blinded. But when he touched the woman's face, her face went back to normal. She was so beautiful, it left a lasting impression on even the apathetic Doma. He mentions she had the same face as Inosuke and concludes she must be his mother.
Doma slashes Inosuke's chest twice creating an X-like mark.
Inosuke says that he has no mother and was raised by boars, to Doma's amusement; "You're a human, so a human must have given birth to you". Inosuke charges forward and readies his Beast Breathing: Sixth Fang, to Kanao's concern, only for Doma to state this encounter is a miracle and simultaneously slash at Inosuke's chest twice creating an X-like mark. He quickly summons more ice and knocks both Demon Slayers into the cult room's pond. As Kanao urges Inosuke to calm down, Doma continues his story. He had no intention of eating the woman, as "having someone beautiful next to you feels pretty good, you know?" Though he considered her unintelligent, she was talented at singing. The woman continually sang a pinky-promise lullaby to her baby, Doma mentioning that she sang with different lyrics each time and adding the song soon became a village song.
Inosuke realizes that pinky promise memory was not because of Shinobu. Doma purely planned on letting her live her life but learned that though she wasn't particularly smart, the woman, named Kotoha, was sharp. She soon learned Doma devoured the followers of the cult. Confronting him for his lies and fleeing the temple, Kotoha apologized to Inosuke, cursing herself for continually making mistakes, going the wrong way and repeatedly saying she was sorry.
Doma calls Kotoha's existence pointless infront of Inosuke and Kanao.
She became lost in the forest and unable to find the human village. Cornered at a cliff's edge, she apologizes once more to Inosuke before dropping him off the cliff into the water. Doma kills her shortly after. He believed the baby would died dropped from the cliff and cried at how sad the situation has become. Inosuke suddenly figures out she was killed, his mother was killed. Doma ate her to the very bone and noted if she went to her husband, he would continue beating her, and if she was alone by herself on the road, she would end up dead as well. Doma mocks Kotoha's life for being so unfortunate, "Was there ever a happy moment in her life?", and calls her existence pointless, causing Kanao to furiously tell him to silence himself. As Inosuke grabs his fallen sword from the water, he remembers his mother's love for him.
Doma comments: "It truly is a miracle, meeting you here". Now filled with rage, Inosuke declares, "The demon who killed his mother and my friends is right before my eyes". He stands up and thanks Doma for letting him remember everything, but voices he won't cut off his head now. He takes a stances and readies to fight Upper Rank Two, declaring that "I'll show you what true hell is like".
Doma tells Inosuke that though he was raised by boars and knows his way with words, he is mistaken. The demon claims heaven and hell don't exist, figments of human fantasies. To him, the humans who live righteously suffer tragedies, while the evil live free to do whatever they want, adding that since divine punishment doesn't exist, mentally weak people therefore believe the evil go to hell upon death. He tells them that they keep this belief deep in their minds and calls humans pitiful. Inosuke decides that instead, he'll create hell for Doma.
Inosuke yells at Doma to get back down so they can continue fighting.
As he charges, telling Doma to stop talking about his mother's life as unfortunate, Doma retaliates with Blood Demon Art: Freezing Clouds. Inosuke uses Beast Breathing, Tenth Fang: Whirling Fangs, rotating his blades to disperse the icy cloud. Kanao attempts to attack Doma from behind but he anticipates it, swiping his fans at her neck. Though she parries the fan, his swipe still knocks her into the water. Doma clings to the roof, causing Inosuke to yell for him to come down and face him. Doma tells them that as Akaza is defeated, he no longer has the time, instead creating ice dolls using Crystalline Divine Child to fight the Demon Slayers.
Doma tells Kanao and Inosuke that the ice dolls are as powerful as him.
As they land, Inosuke and Kanao are confused, but are soon shocked when the dolls use Scattering Lotuses to fight them. Doma tells them the ice dolls are as powerful as him, leaving them to it as he walks away, making Inosuke furious. Kanao tells him to focus on the battle, as a doll uses Frozen Lotus to slash at Inosuke, forcing him back. Doma notices Inosuke isn't breathing in his fog, confusing him. As the dolls use Cold White Princesses and envelopes the room with more fog, Inosuke becomes incensed that everything around him is freezing. Doma is intrigued by him as a fighter he had never face. He decide to force the Demon Slayers to use all their techniques, as information would be useful in future to kill them.
Doma's face began to melting from Shinobu's poison.
As Kanao is forced to hold back another Lotus Vines onslaught, she hopes she and Inosuke can keep Doma inside the room with them for a little longer. However, Doma immediately decide to create a fifth doll to kill the combatants quicker, or face getting scolded. With that, he forges one in his fans and releases it, the doll immediately deploying Wintry Icicles to knock Kanao back further. Soon, Inosuke's arms get slashed by the icy vines, worrying Kanao and telling him to hold out for longer. She herself becomes overwhelmed by the continual slashes of the ice lotuses. Doma overhears her and is confused at how they will survive for any longer. Knowing his dolls will record everything during the battle, he decides to leave.
As Doma opens the door of the cult room, his face begins to melt, confusing him, to Kanao's hope. He collapses to the floor and suddenly thinks back to Shinobu.
In the past, Shinobu and Kanao converse about if they ever encountered Upper Rank Two. Shinobu believes if she encountered him, and Kanao happened to fight alongside her, she would need to be eaten first, shocking her younger sister. Kanao pleads that she and her would fight the demon together, only for Shinobu to respond back by telling her to abandon those thoughts. Though she knows an Upper Rank is as strong as three Hashiras at minimum, according to their late sister Kanae, Upper Two is gluttonous, with an obsession for eating women.
Doma collapsed further from the effect of Shinobu's poison
Shinobu knows if the demon faces a Hashira with great abilities, a body in excellent condition and is a woman, he would definitely eat her, worrying Kanao further. She tells Kanao that her body is currently concentrated with wisteria poison. As Kanao tells her she is also willing to go through the same thing, Shinobu tells her it is impossible to reach her level; she had been absorbing the poison for over a year. Shinobu confesses she was the first to do such a feat, herself unsure of the potential side effects in the future and unsure if her plan would work on an Upper Rank or even Muzan. She states her sword has 50 millilitres of poison, but whatever demon consume her would also consume 37 kilograms worth of poison in her body weight.
Kanao explains to Inosuke that Shinobu's poison is affecting Doma.
Doma collapses further from the effects of Shinobu's poison, his arm falling off, his bones melting and his regeneration failing. He realizes he never felt the poison circulate through him until now. His ice dolls soon fracture and collapse as well, to Inosuke's confusion. Kanao realises Shinobu's poison is working and they now have Doma cornered.
Shinobu tells Kanao she doesn't know even if a life's worth of expertise on poison would work on an Upper Rank Demon. Kagaya Ubuyashiki himself had deemed it impossible but advised her to consult with a demon for further knowledge. Shinobu tells her sister, if the poison did start working, she must never let her guard down still, adding the only sure way to kill Upper Two is severed his neck. She knows she will definitely weaken him and tells Kanao to deal the finishing blow.
Kanao resolves to not let Shinobu's sacrifice be in vain.
Kanao becomes assured she will kill Upper Two and resolves to not let Shinobu's sacrifice be in vain. As she and Inosuke converged on Doma, he summons his final technique: Blood Demon Art: Rime - Water Lily Bodhisattva, forming a massive ice bodhisattva that towers over them. With the two stunned at this new threat, the giant ice figure slams down onto the cult room pond, sending Inosuke and Kanao flying back. Kanao realises if they get forced away from the fog, Doma will have the time to recover, and if they entered the fog and inhaled it, they would no longer be able to fight. However, she notices though Doma's bodhisattva is powerful, it is shoddy; Doma has lost all his precision and creating it was a last ditch effort. She decides to use her own last technique and remembers her last moments with Shinobu.
Kanao remembers Shinobu's warning about the backlash of Final Form: Equinoctial Vermilion Eye.
Shinobu warns her that using the technique might blind her; eyeballs are delicate, with very thin blood vessels and nerves, telling her not to endanger and burden herself by releasing such power. Kanao rejects her warning, asking why should she worry about her vision when Shinobu gave her own life. She calls her sister a sweet and honorable person, declaring she wanted to protect her with her life, and she wanted her, Aoi, Sumi, Kiyo and Naho and herself to all go home together.
Kanao swings her blade at Doma's decaying head.
Kanao activates Flower Breathing: Final Form - Equinoctial Vermillion Eye, causing her eyes to flush full of blood and her perception heightened even further than ever. The giant bodhisattva becomes slow in her eyes; she can see its hand about to slam down. She realises her scleras are turning red and quickly slices up the ice figure's hand to reach Doma. As she swings her katana at Doma's decaying head, the bodhisattva turns back and blasts Kanao with the icy fog, freezing her back and arms. Her sword reaches his neck but she can no longer swing further with her arms stuck frozen. Inosuke sees this and uses a new technique, Sudden Throwing Strike, hurling his blades at Doma.
His swords hit Kanao's, driving the blade through Doma's neck and decapitating him.
Doma is in disbelief at losing to Shinobu, and Kanao, and Inosuke.
Doma is in disbelief at having his head sliced off. He expresses self pity for losing to a sword-wielder who didn't have enough strength to slice off necks, even though he had put much effort into what he believed was for other people's sakes. However, he doesn't give up right away and thinks to himself that he still has a chance and might not die, like Muzan. He also knows Akaza was also to replicate his feat.
However, as his head falls to the floor and bounces, his body begins to disintegrate and he realizes he is going to die. He thinks to himself how he doesn't feel anything, recalling back to a moment in his childhood: his mother had stabbed his father to death after the latter had flirted with numerous female followers, later committing suicide via poison shortly after.
Despite this tragedy, his only thoughts were about ventilating the room; he couldn't comprehend the deaths because of his apathy and was only bothered by the smell of their blood. Doma remembers how he was turned into a demon at the age of 20 and lived over a century, but in the end, human emotions had been alien to him.
In purgatory, Shinobu holds Doma's head in her hand, the former expressing relief at Doma's death. With a smile, she states that she can now be at rest.
