He asks Kanata for how much time until dawn arrives, but when she answers that they still have an hour and a half left, Kiriya's eyes widen with the realization that a lengthy battle still remains.
A Kasugai crow announces to the Demon Slayers that the sun will rise in one and a half hours. Hearing this, Tanjiro remarks that they still have a long time ahead of them and wonders on the whereabouts of everyone else. After spotting the shaken Mitsuri, Obanai beside her, and Giyu nearby pulling himself out of the rubble, he attempts to locate Muzan's scent beneath the castle's remains.
Muzan goads the Hashira into pinning him until dawn.
The mountain of debris suddenly erupts into the air as the Demon King reveals himself; now sporting eight blade-tipped whips on his back, he pushes away the rubble as he remarks about their intentions to hold him until dawn. "If you think you can... then go ahead and try!!" Launching his whips and arms, Muzan instigates his final assault against the Demon Slayer Corps by attacking the Hashira first.
Obanai, Mitsuri, and Giyu barely dodge his blows before they respond by attacking him directly, attempting to use Serpent Breathing, Third Form, Love Breathing, Second Form, and Water Breathing, Eighth Form. Obanai's blade weaves into Muzan's neck and begins to cut through him; despite knowing that decapitation won't kill him, Obanai hopes they can at least break up his body and weaken him that way. However, the Hashira stare at the demon in utter surprise as all of their attacks have seemingly missed their mark.
The Demon Slayers sacrifice themselves to shield the Hashira.
Mitsuri questions if they failed to land a hit, but Giyu soon realizes that they have indeed slashed him; it is Muzan who is regenerating as fast as he is cut. Obanai wonders how they will deal with Muzan if they cannot even damage him, just as Muzan prepares to wipe them out in one blow. To their shock, it is the remaining Demon Slayers who are struck instead, using themselves as human shields to protect them and dying in droves as they block Muzan's attacks.
They charge head-on with the goal of protecting the Hashira and anyone with a chance of harming Muzan; out loud, a Demon Slayer asks how many times the Hashira have saved them, believing they would have died long ago without them and pushing his peers to not hold back. The Hashira grow horrified to see them sacrifice themselves in desperate fashion, while Tanjiro attempts to follow behind them for a chance at attacking Muzan. Suddenly, he coughs blood and stumbles to the ground in pain.
Tanjiro succumbs to Muzan's poisonous blood.
In the midst of attacking, Muzan remarks that those who die quickly are lucky to have done so, and those who aren't immediately kill will follow them even if he touches them; he points the Hashiras' attention to Tanjiro nearby; unmoving and with an expression of agony on his face as a tumour-like mass grows over his slashed eye. As Giyu looks on in horror, the demon explains that he has mixed his blood into his attacks. It will not transform humans into demons and instead acts as a poison to induce cellular destruction and eventually death; he boldly declares, "Tanjiro Kamado is dead."
Nezuko suddenly wakes up, to Sakonji's shock.
As Nezuko lies unconscious, she is stirred by a vision of her father asking her to wake up, claiming that Tanjiro is in danger. She suddenly rises up and stares up in shock, much to Sakonji's confusion. Tengen and Shinjuro then hear a loud crash as Nezuko runs away from her room, with Sakonji attempting to chase after her; the former Hashira questions the demon on where she is going, while Suma is shocked to see she has broken down her doors to escape. Shinjuro informs Kiriya about Nezuko fleeing from them and asks for his next orders.
Kiriya panics at the news and cannot find a solution; Muzan cannot be controlling Nezuko because he is unable to, and if Tamayo's medicine had worked, then Sakonji would have been able to stop her. Just as he is about to order Nezuko to be brought back, he feels the hand of his father on his shoulder, allowing Nezuko to do as she pleases and reassuring his son. Kuina asks the Oyakata on who she can send after her, but Kiriya replies that it is no longer necessary. Kanata questions his intentions, as if a demon captures her, they may never get Nezuko back; Kiriya acknowledges this but tearfully answers that their father had told him to let her go.
Guided by her visions of her father, Nezuko runs through the forest, too quickly for Sakonji to keep up. She soon leaps high into the air and plummets down a cliff, landing down into the trees below safely. Unable to see her anymore, Sakonji is astonished and wonders if Tamayo's medicine has failed, as Nezuko continues to run towards the unconscious Tanjiro on the battlefield.
Muzan injures Mitsuri, Giyu, and Obanai.
As Muzan continues to battle the three Hashira, Giyu realizes he must use a sword from a Demon Slayer who used Water Breathing to keep fighting, while Obanai laments that Muzan is too fast for them. The Demon King begins to land his hits, causing deep cuts in Mitsuri's chest, Giyu's arm and leg, and Obanai's face and arm. As he fights, he expresses surprise to see that they can move with their wounds, believing their marks are making them harder to kill. Seeing she was still struck despite Giyu and Obanai defending her, Mitsuri attempts to keep fighting but collapses when the pain from her injuries flare.
Gyomei saves Mitsuri in the nick of time.
As Muzan's arm closes in on her, Obanai yells at her in vain as she asks that he save himself instead. The demon's arm is suddenly destroyed, narrowly saving the Love Hashira; the other Hashira and Muzan watch as the spiked flail that destroyed it returns to its owner, Gyomei. As he apologizes for his lateness, much to Mitsuri's tearful gratitude, Muzan instantly recognizes him as the Demon Slayer who defeated Kokushibo, just as he is sliced down the middle by the accompanying Wind Hashira.
Sanemi then hurls bottles of oil at the demon, who is soaked in the liquid as he slashes them to pieces, allowing the Hashira to set him alight with a match. Muzan taunts him for using dirty tactics, but Sanemi claims it is what he deserves, vengefully promising to kill him. Appearing out of the Infinity Castle's debris, Murata sees Muzan in the distance; he recognizes him as his family's enemy and moves to try and kill him. Giyu suddenly calls out to him and explains that Tanjiro has been downed, asking that he take him to safety and tends to his wounds.
Shocked by this, Murata quickly rushes over to Tanjiro and begins to carry him away from the battlefield; he grows tearful as he realizes that Giyu has still remembered him from when they fought together in Final Selection. Accepting that the Water Hashira has now advanced far ahead of him, he pushes himself to remain useful, as everyone else has fought hard until the end.
The sky then clears to a bright day. Tanjiro wonders if dawn has already arrived but realizes it is impossible; he also notices his inability to smell anything.
At first, Tanjiro believes the house before him is his own but notices differences that make him sure it isn't. Seeing an axe in his hand, he wonders if he had been chopping wood and if his life is flashing before him. He feels a child holding onto his clothes and addressing him as her father; Tanjiro is unsure if the child is his when he then notices she is pointing towards a tree. In the shade, Yoriichi appears and respectfully bows to him, as Tanjiro realizes he is meeting the man who first used breathing techniques.
Murata attempts to resuscitate Tanjiro as Takeuchi appears.
Murata attempts reviving Tanjiro but to no avail; he is not breathing and his heart is not beating, though with Murata's own loud breathing and heart rate, he cannot tell. He is startled when Takeuchi suddenly calls out to him from behind, thankful to see him. He explains that Yushiro is trapped beneath the rubble and he needs his assistance. Unwilling to leave and let Tanjiro die, Murata is at first hesitant to go, but Takeuchi assures him that if they can save Yushiro, he can in turn treat Tanjiro.
Sitting at Sumiyoshi's house, Yoriichi explains that he needed someone to listen to him, and the only people who came to mind were him and Suyako. Tanjiro wonders if he can ask him about the 13th form when he begins speaking; he remarks that it had been 2 years since they last met and he is glad to see he is well. Tanjiro becomes confused but he continues talking, noting that Sumire was still a baby and has grown much since then. He wonders why he cannot say anything on his mind or move as he wants to, but soon realizes he is seeing his ancestor's memories, and thus has no control over it.
Yoriichi is pleased to see his family well, as when people are happy, it makes him happy. He believes the world is a beautiful place where one is blessed to be born in it.
Yoriichi remembers his mother as a kind woman of deep faith.
His mother was a woman of deep faith, who prayed daily for strife to leave the world. She also prayed to the Sun deity to shine on his ears, as he was believed then to be deaf; she also made him hanafuda charms as earrings. He regretted causing her so much worry when he did not speak. His elder brother was a kind boy who was always concerned about him. One particular day, when Yoriichi played with his brother, their disapproving father struck Michikatsu; he later gave him a handmade flute and asked him to blow it whenever he needed him, telling him not to worry and smiling despite his bruise.
Because he was an unwanted child, Yoriichi left his home when his mother died. Initially supposed to become a priest, he ran away and explored the world beneath the night sky. Despite this, his feet did not tire after an entire day of running. When he came to the mountains, he found a small rice paddy and saw a girl standing in it. She was roughly the same age as him and was carrying a bucket as she stood still. Yoriichi asked her what she was doing, and the girl responded to his question. "My family died in a plague. I'm all alone and very lonely. So I came here to find tadpoles to take him."
Yoriichi begins living with Uta.
She continued to stand unmoving, but as the sun began to set, she freed the tadpoles instead. When asked why she let them go, the girl admitted that she felt sorry about separating them from their families. Yoriichi decided to accompany her home, causing her to turn to him; he saw her eyes were like obsidian. Her name was Uta and they decided to live together. Unlike the quiet Yoriichi, Uta could speak from morning until the evening; it was also during this time that Yoriichi learnt that he saw the world differently to other people, as Uta never knew anyone who could see through the bodies of living things. This epiphany allowed him to understand why he felt disconnected from others; it was as if he was a kite with a severed string, but regardless, Uta held onto him.
Ten years later, the two married and it was about the time Uta was to give birth. To prepare, Yoriichi set out to find a midwife and hoped to return before sundown. Along the way, he came across an old man travelling through the mountains alone. Though he had a weak heart, he was attempting to visit his son after he had been killed in battle. Yoriichi carried the man on his back and travelled to his son's location, deciding to summon the midwife tomorrow instead. He hurried home as night fell, but by the time he arrived, someone had killed Uta and their unborn child.
Yoriichi laments the existence of demons and the pain they cause.
As Tanjiro listens to his harrowing story, Yoriichi remarked, "There are those who will not hesitate to trample upon someone whose life is more precious to you than your own." For ten days, he sat in a daze as he held his wife's body, only brought out of his catatonic state when a Demon Slayer arrived. He had been pursuing the demon and encouraged Yoriichi to mourn his family properly. As he buried his family and prayed for them, Yoriichi reminisces on his resolve to keep pushing on past their deaths.
"My dream was to live a quiet life with my family in a small house where we would sleep side by side. I would be close enough to see the beloved faces of my wife and child and close enough to reach out and take their hands. That would have been enough. But even that did not come true. Demons exist in this beautiful world."
The advent of the five fundamental Breathing Styles.
He became a Demon Slayer and learnt that though humanity had always been hunting demons, they did so without using breathing techniques; he subsequently taught them. Within the Demon Slayer Corps, the best amongst them were known as the Hashira, and atop their own swordsmanship skill, learning the Breathing Styles that lead to the advent of Flame, Wind, Water, Thunder, and Stone Breathing allowed them to become even more powerful. The Demon Slayers began killing demons one after another; Yoriichi also adds that after demons had killed his subordinates, Michikatsu too became a Demon Slayer.
Soon after this, Yoriichi encountered the progenitor of all demons as he was accompanied by a girl. The moment they met, Yoriichi understood that he was born with the sole purpose of defeating him.
Upon encountering the progenitor of demons, Yoriichi immediately sensed his violent intent, describing him as an erupting volcano whose boiling magma threatened to consume everything. Muzan only spoke to him about his disinterest in swordsmen who used breathing techniques; the moment he stopped speaking, he suddenly lashed out and tried to kill him with his bladed arms. Yoriichi ducked below the attack and saw his fearsome speed and long reach. As he heard the bamboo splitting and falling behind him, he sensed that even one scratch could kill him and believed it was the first time he felt a chill down his spine.
Yoriichi overpowers Muzan in an instant.
Seeing inside Muzan, he discovered the demon had seven hearts and five brains, and in that moment, he was able to complete his sword forms. In a single attack, he cuts through Muzan's vital organs at once and dismembers his body; hearing this, Tanjiro wonders if the 13th form is part of his completed forms, wishing Yoriichi would teach him.
Muzan looked on with confusion as his body failed to regenerate, holding his head as he tries to reattach it. Yoriichi knew that his bright red blade would work on even the demon progenitor but he needed to know something about him. "What is the value of a life to you?", he asked, but the angered demon only looked to him without speaking. His reddening face made him believe his words didn't reach him. He noticed the demon girl nearby but saw that she wasn't attempting to help him. With eyes wide open, she simply stared at him and waited; it was as if her eyes were shining with a sense of hope.
Muzan's body explodes, as Yoriichi attempts to destroy all of the pieces.
Yoriichi decided to kill the demon progenitor first, but as he steps forth, he heard the sound of teeth grinding. The dismembered body suddenly bursts into hundreds of pieces, and caught off-guard, Yoriichi only managed to destroy slightly more than 1,500 of the 1,800 he saw. What remained was too small to be cut and he estimates that what escaped was enough to make a head-sized lump of flesh. As he stood still, the girl collapsed and began to cry, lamenting that despite Yoriichi's near victory, the demon managed to overcome his decapitation. She tore at her hair as she angrily yelled, "I wish that filthy man died!! Muzan Kibutsuji!!"
She then stopped and looked at herself, wondering why she was not dead. Yoriichi calmed and approached the girl, and she quickly spoke to him about Muzan; he was the demons' progenitor and he was likely to never reveal himself to him again. The girl was relieved to be free of his control due to his weakened state; when Yoriichi asked for her help, she showed initial hesitance but eventually agreed. Her name was Tamayo and he noted that she had sad eyes; Tanjiro is shocked to learn this about Tamayo. Suddenly, he heard from the Demon Slayers running to him that Michikatsu had become a demon.
Yoriichi is banished for failing to kill Muzan, Tamayo, and Michikatsu becoming a demon.
As the angered Hashira admonished him in the Ubuyashiki estate, Yoriichi was confronted by his failure to kill Muzan and Tamayo and Michikatsu's transformation. He was banished, but when some demanded that he commit seppuku as well, their Oyakata did not allow it; Yoriichi was sorry to further burden a six year old who had just lost his father. As Sumiyoshi attempts to reassure him, Yoriichi laments his failure to kill Muzan. "I think... I was born with special strength for the purpose of defeating Muzan Kibutsuji. But I was lacking. In the end, I failed. Because of that many more people will die. And that pains me."
Tanjiro is rendered speechless by Yoriichi's retelling of his life; with so much that had happened to him, he cannot find any words to offer. He hopes that Sumiyoshi would say something, but both merely sat in silence for some time. As he tries to find a way to help his hurt friend, Sumire approaches Yoriichi from behind and asks for a hug. Flustered, Sumiyoshi gently asks if he could carry her, as she enjoys it and he is taller than him, and without speaking, Yoriichi holds Sumire and lifts her up.
Yoriichi hugs Sumire in an emotional breakdown.
The little girl squeals with happiness, causing Yoriichi to break down in tears. Suyako soon returns from gathering chestnuts in the forest, only to see Sumiyoshi standing beside Yoriichi as he tearfully hugs Sumire. Seeing it is her friend, Suyako reassures Yoriichi and invites him inside for a meal, asking him to cheer up. Watching the scene unfold, Tanjiro acknowledges that he is in the middle of a battle and that Yoriichi had died hundreds of years ago.
"But... I can't help but wish that his heart will find even a little peace."
After a series of attacks from Muzan, Gyomei comments on how he appears to be getting faster, so fast that the Mitsuri barely manages to dodge his attacks on pure intuition and luck.
Mitsuri mortally wounded by Muzan's attack.
Mitsuri, before she can land an attack, realizes that she's getting dragged down by one of Muzan's arms. Another attack from him manages to slice some of the Hashira's right cheek off and injure the shoulder of her right arm. Obanai jumps to rescue her, and with the help of Sanemi, Giyu and Gyomei holding Muzan back, he's able to carry her to another Demon Slayer.
He commands him to find Yushiro to treat her injuries and the Slayer agrees. However, Mitsuri insists on keep fighting but Obanai doesn't allow her. As he leaves her, she pleads him to not die.
Obanai, as he's running contemplates the number of people that have died, all because of the existence of demons. At first, wishes that he and Mitsuri had met under normal circumstances, but takes it back saying that he would rather die (after killing Muzan that is) and cleanse himself of the filthy bloodline he carries within him. His bandages, fall behind him as he's running to reveal slits across his cheeks.
His family stole money and lived a luxurious life from it. Obanai was the first male born in the clan in over 370 years and was confined to a cell because of this. He would have died earlier if it wasn't for his heterochromia, as the demon living there (who ate offsprings in return of the humans living there), with the lower body of a serpent, decided that he should grow a more satisfying size before she'd eat him. She was also the one who ordered the other females of the clan to cut the sides of his mouth to resemble her.
Obanai is saved by Shinjuro.
During this, Obanai manages to steal a hairpin and was able to slowly cut away the wooden cage with it and escape, Kaburamaru, strayed inside the cell before their escape. Because of him, the serpent demon killed everyone else in the clan, and tried to kill Obanai but Shinjuro Rengoku, the Flame Hashira at the time cut her head off, saving Obanai and his female cousin, who threw a fit at him.
By becoming a Demon Slayer, he felt as though he became a better person, even if the souls of the dead family members always dragged him down.
Obanai restates that he would like to die by killing Muzan to purify his blood and hopes to meet Mitsuri again in another life without demons if he and her are ever reincarnated into humans, and, if that happens, he'll confess his love to her.
Nezuko Kamado continues to run towards the location of the battle as a group of Kakushi attempt to keep the site of the battle clear of civilians and redirect all approaching people to evacuate, telling them that they are a rescue team sent by the local policemen.
Another group of Kakushi examine the rubble of the buildings destroyed as a result of Muzan Kibutsuji's attack and find that no one had been harmed due to the damage except for a cat trapped in the rubble. They free it and find that it has a bag strapped to it, as it is none other than Tamayo's cat and it immediately runs off to the battle scene with it's cargo in tow.
Over at the fight, Obanai Iguro and Sanemi Shinazugawa battle Muzan at close quarters and Obanai chops off one of Muzan's arms, cleverly kicking it away as he severed it to prevent the Demon from regenerating immediately. Muzan notes this strategy as well but is unconcerned, saying that the extra time the Demon Slayer has bought is but a blink.
Muzan attacks Obanai with his whip and the Hashira rues all the energy he is having to waste just to avoid the mouths on the whips. He assuredly thinks that he will only allow himself to faint one second after dawn as every second is precious and had been bought for them with the very lives of all the members of the Demon Slayer Corps.
Obanai and Gyomei deflecting Muzan's attacks, thus saving Giyu's life.
Giyu Tomioka begins to weaken as a result of the venom he has received from all of Muzan's attacks and his sword is whipped away from him by a whip. Both Obanai and Gyomei Himejima intervene and slice it, with Sanemi grabbing his sword and throwing it near the Water Hashira and yells at him to focus and or else he will kill him. Giyu gratefully grabs the sword and performs the Water Breathing, Third Form: Flowing Dance resolving not to back down and to keep fighting till the very end.
Muzan admits that they are more resilient than he had expected but is unconcerned as it is only a matter of time before his venom kills them all, long before dawn. The Hashira continue to struggle against Muzan as the poison continues to weaken them until suddenly Tamayo's cat jumps onto the scene and ejects it's cargo: vials of antidotes to Muzan's poison. It manages to fire all the vials at the Hashira and they immediately begin to inject the antidote into them as Muzan slices the cat into pieces.
Chachamaru delivers the antidotes.
Sanemi smiles as he notices his tumors vanish and Gyomei also notices his own frenzied pulse and constant pain vanish and the Hashira are able to fight with more ease again which Sanemi is thankful for. Gyomei notes that it is possibly just a temporary cure for the symptoms but that they are fortunate for such an event to occur. Muzan quickly deduces what had happened and realises it was Tamayo's doing, cursing her for being a thorn in his side even in death. With immense fury, he launches a frenzied attack that creates multiple craters in the landscape ahead of him.
Obanai's blade turns bright red as his Demon Slayer Mark appears.
The Hashira all barely manage to dodge the attacks as Obanai wistfully thinks to himself how his contribution has been the lowest, wishing he could land more crucial blows. Thinking that when one's life is in danger one is able to exert explosive strength, he reflects back on how before he had never lifted anything heavier than a pair of chopsticks and his biggest task was escaping a prison cell.
He could not believe it himself when he had successfully done so and thinks to what Muichiro Tokito did in his final battle against Kokushibo by changing the color of his sword and that according to the crows all he would have been able to do was grip his sword tightly.
Saying he had been shocked when he heard about it and at first believed it had changed color due to a rise in temperature. However, now he realised that to obtain a bright red blade he would have to grip his sword with all his might and Obanai grits his teeth as he puts all his strength into gripping his sword and it begins to turn bright red.
Obanai Iguro reflects on how upon seeing the bright red blade he also started to see stars in his peripheral vision and realized he had made a mistake. Recognizing that he had been too fixated on tightening his grip on his sword and gaining the bright red blade that he had been close to passing out due to lack of oxygen.
He is brought back to earth with a yell from Sanemi Shinazugawa who warns him to watch out as Muzan Kibutsuji has launched an attack his way. Noting that if even one of them falls it will increase the burden on the others Obanai tries to stand up and fight, willing himself to make up for Mitsuri Kanroji's absence as well.
Giyu seeing Obanai in mid-air having successfully dodged Muzan's attack.
However, he has lost sensation in all parts of his body except for his sword hand. Giyu Tomioka attempts to intercept Muzan's attack but he isn't able to outpace the Demon's blow. Suddenly, he looks up and sees Obanai up in the air having successfully dodged the attack.
Muzan unveils his invisible attackers
Muzan sees this and attempts to attack him in midair but is shocked to see the Serpent Hashira dodge it easily again. Further surprised at his right arm and whips being cut off seemingly from nowhere, Muzan notices that it is an odd kind of cut that could not have been made by the weapons of those he is fighting.
Forcibly regrowing his severed limb with a delay, Muzan then resumes his attack to stop Gyomei Himejima and Sanemi from getting in too close on him. He is further surprised as his left arm is chopped off as a result of a similarly mysterious cut, Muzan deduces that it has to be from a blade with jagged edges and realizes that someone else is present who is also aiming to destroy him.
Obanai shocks Muzan and cuts off his arms.
Quickly assessing this new threat, Muzan analyzes his surroundings, saying that even if a spell from Tamayo's Demon could make someone invisible, it couldn't erase traces of their existence. Though he is unable to see any silhouettes through the dust clouds Muzan is still able to hear the air parting in some areas. Deducing that there are three hidden attackers around him he slices at their approximate locations and is able to land a hit on all three of them.
Inosuke Hashibira, Kanao Tsuyuri and Zenitsu Agatsuma suddenly pop into view as some seals placed on their heads get sliced off by Muzan's attacks. They are taken aback at how quickly he was able to find them out but Gyomei is pleasantly surprised to notice them all still alive as Inosuke boasts he wouldn't die and that he had plenty of seals to spare.
The Hashira turn their blades bright red.
Muzan unceremoniously interrupts Inosuke's monologue and swipes at him with a whip but his attention is drawn back to himself mid-attack as Obanai slices off both of his arms. He is displeased at the time it takes his arms to regrow from these attacks by a bright red blade and Sanemi is heartened as he notes this fact to his companions.
Kanao and Zenitsu hurriedly put on new seals and attack Muzan with Flower Breathing, Fourth Form: Crimson Hanagoromo and Thunder Breathing, First Form: Thunderclap and Flash. Enraged, Muzan calls them a bunch of pesky flies, saying they have nothing but pitiful tricks but is interrupted by Obanai who attacks him with the Serpent Breathing, Third Form: Coil Choke.
Gyomei thinks to himself that this addition to their numbers and Obanai manifesting a bright red blade has helped them and it also allows him to concentrate more. The Stone Hashira clangs his weapons together and upon impact both of them change color to bright red before swinging at Muzan and knocking off his entire left shoulder, exposing his spine.
The Demon pauses and Sanemi yells Giyu to prepare himself as he swings his blade at Giyu's, turning both of their weapons bright red as well. A crow arrives overhead and announces that dawn will break in one hour and three minutes and Sanemi declares that there is no problem as they will chop Muzan into pieces.
Yushiro injects Tanjiro Kamado multiple times with the antidote to Muzan's poison made by Tamayo to try and rejuvenate him, as the Demon Slayers around him ask if injecting Tanjiro so many times is safe for him. He quietens them and says that his condition since it's been some time since Muzan struck him.
The Demon Slayers try to free Tanjiro's katana from his hands but fail as he has a very tight grip on it, Yushiro takes this as a sign that Tanjiro still has the will to fight and suddenly the Demon Slayer holding Tanjiro's head yells out saying that he felt his pulse return.
Yushiro, Murata and Takeuchi attempting to wake Tanjiro up

The Hashira are knocked unconscious.
Back at the fight with Muzan, a Kakushi hidden out of sight peers over to see how things are faring and gets hope that they might hold out until dawn. Gyomei Himejima cleaves off the left half of Muzan's torso as Sanemi Shinazugawa rushes over to a pile of seals on the ground and puts one on his forehead.
As soon as he puts it on he is able to see Kanao Tsuyuri, Zenitsu Agatsuma and Inosuke Hashibira as the latter declares he wants a bright red blade like the Hashira as well, Sanemi launches the Wind Breathing, Seventh Form: Gale, Sudden Gusts towards Muzan.
Tanjiro saves Kanao with the Hinokami Kagura: Beneficent Radiance.
Gyomei is relieved at the arrival of the new fighters as that allowed him to concentrate more, looking into the Transparent World, he sees that Muzan has multiple hearts and brains and thus will not die if they chop off his head, he also notes that they move around inside his body making it difficult to strike them.
An idea suddenly strikes him, believing that if the others could also see Muzan in the transparent world then they would be able to strike the organs simultaneously and destroy Muzan for good. He calls out to the others to look closely at Muzan's body and see if their vision changes and if they can see through him, for an instant Obanai Iguro is able to do so and is shocked at the phenomenon.
"It's hard to tell which one of us is the Demon."
He doesn't have long to ponder on this however, as Muzan launches a devastating attack in all directions and crushes everything around him, flinging everyone into their surroundings. The hidden Kakushi is shocked at the sound and looks over again to see what had happened and is dumbfounded as he sees Muzan standing on his own and the surrounding area having sustained heavy damage.
Looking right next to him he is even more baffled as he sees Gyomei knocked into the building he is hiding behind and that he has lost a leg. His horror only grows as he sees that Sanemi has been flung into the upper storey of a tall building while Obanai, Zenitsu and Inosuke are all unconscious in the rubble and Giyu Tomioka's sword arm has been severed.

Yoriichi performs Sun Breathing: Thirteenth Form at Suyako's request.

Saying he noticed wasted movement in the variation of the angle of his wrist, differences in footwork and the interval between breaths. Sumiyoshi Kamado made sure to memorize all of them, searing them into his memory, left breathless at the beauty of the movements. When he finished demonstrating, Suyako and the children were overflowing with excitement and Yoriichi bowed his head in embarrassment.
Yoriichi's smile.

In the present, Tanjiro stands in front of Muzan Kibutsuji and thanks Yoriichi for his actions. Tanjiro plans to attack Muzan by connecting all the forms together and continue to strike his brains and hearts until dawn.
Tanjiro's resemblance to Yoriichi angers Muzan.

Tanjiro commences Sun Breathing: Thirteenth Form against Muzan.

Unfazed, Tanjiro says he will connect all the forms as that's how they were designed to be and resolves to succeed.
Muzan Kibutsuji notes he is well aware that living creatures are able to tap into reserves of strength unbeknownst to them to escape death and looks on to see Tanjiro Kamado doing the same in his attempt to connect all twelve Forms of the Sun Breathing. He sees that Tanjiro has turned his blade bright red as well, just as the other Hashira had but is unconcerned as he says that the young Demon Slayer's attacks are nowhere near as powerful as those of Yoriichi Tsugikuni.
Tanjiro successfully connects six forms of the Sun Breathing.

Beginning to feel fatigued, Tanjiro heaves and slows down but he keeps telling himself to focus on one second while connecting the Sun Breathing: Fake Rainbow and Burning Bones, Summer Sun.
Muzan notices Tanjiro's attacks begin to lose their accuracy and surmises that he will soon lose his red blade as well, saying that he is yet another swordsman who would never live up to Yoriichi nor reproduce the terrifying technique the old swordsman had used against him.
Tamayo reveals the poison has another effect.
